In the Eyes of a Beauty: The Current State of the Japanese Aviation Industry (II) 73

The history of the Japanese Army's aviation predates that of the Navy. In 1910, Lieutenant Tokugawa (now promoted to Major General and Principal of the Army Flying School) brought back an Henri Farman biplane from France. This marked the beginning of military aircraft imports, and he was also Japan's first aviator. In the same year, Major Hino brought back a Grade monoplane with 25 horsepower from Germany, and flew it at the Yoyogi training ground in Tokyo on December 19, 1910. These two aircraft were the first military aircraft of the Japanese Army. The following year, a Rad biplane and a Pralia monoplane were purchased. In 1912, the Army Flying School was established. In the same year, Major General Tokugawa personally copied a biplane equipped with a Gnome engine and flew it between Tokyo and Tokorozawa. Since then, Japanese-made military aircraft have gradually appeared. In 1913, two Maurice Farman biplanes (Renault 70 horsepower) and one Nieuport monoplane (50 horsepower) were purchased from France. Soon after, the Army adopted the Farman aircraft as the standard model and manufactured it at the Army factory using Japanese materials. This Maurice Farman type is the Nakajima-manufactured biplane, equipped with a 150-horsepower Hall-Scott engine, and used in the Army flying squadrons. During the European War, Japan only dispatched one army corps to attack Qingdao and sent some aviators to the Western Front. However, at that time, it was considered that there was a lack of practical experience. After the war ended, in order to remedy the deficiencies, Colonel Foulques, a famous French Air Force officer, was invited to Japan to teach. The progress of the Japanese flying squadrons today is entirely due to the French. After the war, a large number of British and French aircraft were purchased again. The first Army fighter jets were imported from France in 1922, namely SPAD S.XIII and Nieuport 29C (300 horsepower). Later, the Nakajima Aircraft Manufacturing Plant copied many Nieuport models. Since 1925, the standard of aircraft used by the Army has been the Salmson 230-horsepower reconnaissance aircraft manufactured by Kawasaki and the Army Factory (total weight 2552 pounds, maximum speed 112 miles, climb speed to 3300 feet in 4 minutes, to 9800 feet in 13 minutes 10 seconds, endurance 3 hours), and the Nakajima-made Ise-Hispano 300-horsepower fighter aircraft (total weight 2552 pounds, maximum speed 130 miles, climb speed to 3300 feet in 3 minutes 20 seconds, to 9800 feet in 10 minutes 50 seconds). The following is a list of the main types of aircraft currently used by the Japanese Navy.

The Japanese Army Aviation Department has been working very hard on inspecting aircraft performance and research over the years, and is particularly interested in large all-metal bombers. In 1927, the Kawasaki factory manufactured an aircraft equipped with two Kawasaki Tern-Dornier 450-horsepower BMW engines, which has been adopted by the Army. Other aircraft, such as the light bomber with a Nakajima-made biplane and an Ise-Hispano 450-horsepower engine manufactured by Mitsubishi Aircraft Co., Ltd., are also considered to have excellent performance. The performance of the aircraft currently used in the Army airfields is as follows:

(1) Kawasaki Ternier heavy bomber, equipped with two Kawasaki BMW 450-horsepower engines (weight 9680 pounds, total weight 16823 pounds, maximum speed 106 miles, climb speed to 3300 feet in 10 minutes 55 seconds, to 9800 feet in 44 minutes 10 seconds, endurance 5 hours)

(2) Mitsubishi-made light bomber, equipped with an Ise-Hispano 450-horsepower engine (weight 4088 pounds, total weight 7320 pounds, maximum speed 112 miles, climb speed to 3300 feet in 9 minutes 50 seconds, 9800 feet in 56 minutes 45 seconds, endurance 3 hours)

In 1928, the Army Flying Squad held a flying competition. The Ishikawa-jima T-3 biplane (Kawasaki BMW 450 horsepower), the Nakajima N-35 (Nakajima Lorraine 650 horsepower), the Mitsubishi biplane (Mitsubishi Ise-Hispano 450 horsepower), the Kawasaki Type 88 biplane (Kawasaki BMW 450 horsepower), etc., were combined for reconnaissance and bombing battles. The Kawasaki aircraft was the most outstanding, so the Type 88 reconnaissance bomber was adopted. This Kawasaki aircraft is equipped with a Kawasaki BMW 450-horsepower engine. It is an all-metal biplane with the following performance (weight 3872 pounds, total weight 6270 pounds, maximum speed 124 miles, minimum speed 59 miles, climb speed to 3300 feet in 4 minutes 50 seconds, to 9800 feet in 15 minutes 45 seconds, to 16400 feet in 35 minutes 15 seconds, endurance 4-5 hours). It has been modified many times since then, becoming the Type 88-2, and its performance is even greater. In 1930, a Japanese-initiated fighter competition was held, and the Nakajima-made monoplane (Cubitt 450 horsepower) was adopted as the Type 90 fighter. In 1932, the Kawashima-made biplane (500 horsepower Kawasaki BMW engine) was adopted as the Type 92 fighter. In the same year, the Mitsubishi monoplane light reconnaissance aircraft (Mitsubishi Argyle 420 horsepower) was adopted as the standard aircraft. The Japanese Army Air Force now has a supply of domestically produced aircraft, and its air power can gradually compete with the world. Recently, during the Manchurian Incident, taking advantage of China's lack of air force equipment, it greatly exerted its power. According to the Army's current [preparation for patriotism], the latest Type 1933 two-seater fighters and liaison aircraft are currently being urgently manufactured by private companies entrusted by the military. Mitsubishi Aircraft Manufacturing Co., Ltd. is also imitating the Junkers G.38 all-metal super heavy bomber in order to strengthen the first line of air defense, but its contents are not detailed. The following is a list of the general outline of the first-class aircraft currently in use by the Japanese Army.

Chairman Chiang Strictly Prohibits the Army from Press-Ganging 74

Nanchang Communication: Chairman Chiang believes that the army's press-ganging is most likely to arouse public resentment, and has repeatedly issued orders to strictly prohibit it. However, there are still several armies that knowingly violate the ban. He has issued another order to the Commanders-in-Chief of the various routes to suppress bandits to relay the order to all departments and strictly prohibit it. The original order is as follows: [For your obedience, it is found that forced press-ganging is most likely to arouse popular resentment and hinder military operations, and has been strictly prohibited in the past. Recently, according to reports from the county magistrates and inspectors of various counties, the various armies and units still often engage in press-ganging, or change the method to forcibly ask local governments to provide a certain number of laborers, which often makes local governments unable to cope and have to send police to forcibly press-gang. In this situation, although the press-ganging comes from the local government, the resentment is still directed at the army, which is extremely detrimental to the suppression of bandits and has a great impact. If this is not changed drastically, the future danger is unbearable to describe. Therefore, I reiterate my stern warning that hereafter, whether in the process of suppressing or clearing bandits, the troops can only use the original laborers. If there are not enough, they can only carry less baggage or have soldiers help with transportation. Press-ganging is absolutely not allowed, and no means are allowed to be changed to forcibly instruct others to carry out press-ganging. Anyone who violates this will be punished according to military law to serve as a warning. Furthermore, these incidents are often committed by lower-ranking officers, and higher-ranking officers are negligent in detecting them, resulting in the deterioration of military discipline and public resentment. The various senior and middle-ranking officers are still ignorant, which is far from the main point of my repeated instructions to see, speak, act, and move. The harm is extreme. As for the political training personnel of the various units, they have the responsibility of connecting military-civilian feelings, assisting local governments, and reducing public suffering. If the various units do not abide by military discipline and harass the people, they should immediately conduct a detailed investigation, take responsibility for stopping them, and secretly report to this headquarters for verification and handling. Local governments, in the face of national crisis, can also report the matter to senior officers as much as possible, and should not protect their positions and engage in practices that harm the people. In addition to separate orders, this order is hereby issued for your obedience and relay to your subordinates. Be sure to obey this order.]

Henan Province, Fengqiu and Chenliu Request Disaster Relief. Disaster Situation is Also Severe in Both Counties. Disaster Victims Have No Clothes or Food. 75

Kaifeng Communication: This year, the Yellow River has caused harm. In Henan Province, the most severely affected counties are Hua County, Kaocheng, Lanfeng, and Wen County. Few people pay attention to Fengqiu and Chenliu, which are relatively lightly affected counties. Now it is deep autumn, and the people in the disaster areas have no clothes or food. Although the government has repeatedly stated that it will provide emergency relief, it is only a drop in the bucket, and it is difficult to keep them alive. In addition, the epidemic has recurred, and the people are living in dire straits. Every day, there are several requests to the provincial relief association for relief and medicine. The petitions from Fengqiu and Chenliu counties are recorded as follows:

Fengqiu Requests Construction Relief 76

The construction relief methods proposed by Fengqiu County: (1) Digging ditches. It is found that there are three old ditches in the county, namely Wenyang, Tianran, and Zhiju. The Wenyang ditch starts from Sanlizhuang in the northwest of the county, connects with the ditch in Yanjiin County, and ends at the Zhifang Cliff in Changyuan County in the northeast, with a total length of more than 60 li. The Tianran ditch starts from the DaCunji in the west of the county, connects with the Yangwu ditch, and enters the Wenyang ditch at the RanGuzhuang north of the city, with a total length of more than 30 li. The Zhiju ditch starts from the XiaoSunzhuang in the southwest of the county and enters the Tianran ditch at the Sangcun north of the county, with a total length of more than 40 li. There are 13 important bridges on the upstream and downstream of each ditch. All of them have been silted up due to years of disrepair, the channels are blocked, and the bridges have collapsed. Once there is accumulated water, there is nowhere to discharge, and it floods and causes disasters. It is proposed to recruit disaster victims to the three ditches and provide construction relief separately to dig and repair the bridges, a total of 13, to facilitate travel. It is found that the total length of each ditch is more than 130 li. Each li requires 300 workers, and each worker is paid 30 cents a day, totaling 10,700 yuan in relief funds. Each of the 13 bridges requires 10,000 bricks, and the labor cost is 30 yuan. Each brick costs 1 cent, totaling 100 yuan. The total cost of labor and materials for each bridge is 130 yuan. The 13 bridges require a total of 1,690 yuan. The total calculation above requires 12,390 yuan, which can accommodate 5,000 disaster victims. It is requested to start construction relief quickly to provide relief and eliminate floods. (2) Repairing the city and digging moats, repairing and reinforcing dikes. It is found that Fengqiu County City has been in disrepair for a long time. The city towers, city shrines, city parapets, and foundations have many defects and collapses. Pedestrians enter and exit as if walking on flat ground. The moats outside the city have all been silted up. The protective embankment has also been damaged due to years of construction. In 1930, the garrison dug trenches all over the embankment, which was bumpy and uneven, causing further damage. If it is not repaired, it will not be enough for defense. Now is the year of famine, the atmosphere of bandits is restless, and floods occur frequently, so it cannot be regarded as a slow plan. It has been carefully estimated that repairing the city embankment and digging the city moat will require 8,000 yuan in relief funds, to provide relief through construction, which can achieve several benefits at once. (3) Establishing factories. It is found that Fengqiu is a remote small town, and most people are engaged in agriculture. Once there is a natural disaster, they are almost helpless. They do not pay attention to crafts, and there are many idle people. Now is the autumn of commercial warfare, and crafts should be the foundation. Without paying attention to crafts, there is no way to save the people's livelihood. It is proposed to establish factories, hire male and female technicians, and divide them into dyeing, weaving, woodworking, bamboo work, grass hat braiding, soap, and candle making. Recruit young men and women from the disaster victims, and learn by category. In the present time, construction relief can be provided. In the long term, industry can be developed, and everyone can be self-reliant in the future, and there will be fewer idle people. As the saying goes, [It is better to have a skill than to have millions of family assets]. It is not an exaggeration. It is estimated that the purchase of machinery, materials, and office expenses will require about 10,000 yuan.

Chenliu Requests Allocation of Disaster Relief Funds 77

Chenliu County submitted a document stating, [I have secretly investigated that the fourth district of this county, which is located within the Yellow River embankment, has suffered a severe flood, submerging more than ten villages, destroying hundreds of acres of farmland, and flooding no less than two hundred people. The houses buried are estimated to be in the tens of thousands. All of these miserable situations have been truthfully reported by the former Executive Committee, and the council approved and transferred the matter to the Henan Province Relief Association for verification and handling. The county government has also approved the provincial committee to re-investigate the cases. It is reasonable to wait for the implementation of relief, how can there be room for repeated appeals? However, thousands of bereaved people in the disaster area are exposed to the wind and dew, and cannot withstand the cold and hunger. Due to the mixed atmosphere, there has been an outbreak of epidemics. The sick are still under the open sky, and those who are hungry are pale and emaciated. All the so-called disasters of soldiers, bandits, drought, and locusts do not have such a miserable appearance. All the needs of rice, grain, and miscellaneous items have been swept away by the east. The remaining old and weak are only breathing. Only a breath remains, and they are still hoping to continue their lives. Although the headquarters has discussed with the county government and various agencies to raise 90 stones of relief grain in advance, and rushed to the area to distribute emergency relief, the average distribution is less than two liters per person, which is equivalent to a value of less than one cent. It is a drop in the bucket, and it is difficult to help. The righteous grain and benevolent soup are urgently awaited to be issued. Therefore, I once again request the council to reply to the flood relief agency and quickly allocate relief funds and medicine to expand the relief. The gratitude of the disaster victims will not be in vain. (October 2nd)

Shaanxi Province is Building the Highways Connecting Henan, Hubei, and Gansu 78

—The Department of Construction Has Planned and Surveyed—

Xi'an Communication: The Shaanxi Provincial Government previously received a telegram from Chairman Chiang instructing it to construct the Xilao Highway (from Xi'an to Laohekou), which connects this province to Hubei and Henan, and the Fenglong Highway (from Feng County to Malu Town in Long County), which connects this province to Longnan. It was ordered that the Department of Construction should first conduct surveys and designs. The Department of Construction has now drafted an outline for the organization of the survey team and a budget for survey and mapping fees, and submitted them to the provincial government for approval and allocation of funds in order to actively carry out the work. The original presentation stated, [In accordance with your government's Order No. 1580, Chairman Chiang sent a secret telegram ordering the construction of highways in this province connecting Gansu, Hubei, and Henan. We are ordered to provide detailed plans and surveys. While we were complying with the order, we received your government's Order No. 1644, which stated, 'For your compliance, it is found that at the 24th meeting of the committee of this government, the chairman proposed that highways in this province connecting Gansu, Hubei, and Henan should be quickly planned in detail, surveyed on the ground, and funds should be raised for the survey first. The decision was made to hand it over to the Department of Construction to first survey the two roads from Xi'an to Laohekou and from Xi'an to the border of Southern Gansu, and to draw up a plan and estimate the survey expenses and submit them for review, etc., as recorded in the minutes. I have investigated this case and found that I previously received a telegram from Chairman Chiang, which I have complied with and reported back to the Department of Construction for compliance. Therefore, I urgently order the department to immediately comply, quickly conduct surveys on the two roads mentioned above, formulate a plan for the dirt road and several roads separately, and estimate the survey expenses and submit them for review in a consolidated case. This is for your observation and decision. In accordance with this, I have found that the section of the highway connecting Gansu and Qingshui in this province is more important. This road is 270 li long, and the budget requires 500 yuan for survey and start-up expenses, and 5,652.5 yuan for survey and mapping expenses, totaling 6,152.5 yuan. It will take two and a half months to complete. In addition, the main road connecting this province to Hubei is the Xijing Road, which starts from Xi'an, passes through Lantian, Shang County, Shangluo, and reaches Jingziguan, with a total length of 660 li. The budget requires 500 yuan for survey and start-up expenses, and 12,453.5 yuan for survey and mapping expenses, totaling 12,953.5 yuan. It will take five and a half months to complete. Before the actual survey is conducted, it is difficult to accurately design the project. A detailed design should be made after the actual survey. In accordance with the order, I have drafted an outline for the organization of the survey team and a budget for survey and mapping fees, and submitted them for your approval and allocation of funds for actual measurement, which is for the public good.] The outline of the survey team's organization is omitted. (September 21st)

Zhejiang Department of Construction Pays Attention to Improving Industry 79

—Implementing a Unified Policy to Improve Sericulture—

—Improving Cotton Industry and Breeding Millions of Cotton Seeds—

Zhejiang Province has always been an agricultural area, but in recent years, the province's annual output of grains and wheat has been less than 24 million dan, and the output of cotton has been less than 600,000 dan, which has a significant impact on people's food and clothing. Even sericulture, which has a good reputation, is also declining. The rural economy is increasingly declining, and the industrial and commercial sectors are also in danger. In view of this, the Department of Construction has taken separate measures to improve and promote it. The following is an overview of its work in recent years.

Revitalizing Agriculture 80

For the improvement of agriculture, the Department of Construction formed an agricultural committee last summer, invited experts to study, and set up a training institute for agricultural extension workers in Wenjiayan, Xiaoshan this spring to train agricultural extension workers in various counties, encourage people to afforest, and promote bee keeping, horse raising, sheep raising, and the protection of cattle and other sideline occupations. These are all active work. A Bureau of Entomology was established to take charge of pest control, and a training institute for pest control personnel was established to train pest control personnel. In addition, in order to address the damage to rice and wheat caused by farmers' unlimited use of chemical fertilizers, a management office was established to ban it. These are all passive work. The more important of its active works are the following:

Improving Sericulture 81

In view of the decline of sericulture, the Department of Construction urged the sericulture farm to produce high-quality original seeds, supervised private seed farms to produce non-toxic silkworm seeds, and banned native species. In the autumn of last year, the first model area for improving sericulture was established in Nansha, Xiaoshao, to promote excellent varieties and guide farmers to raise autumn silkworms. This year, a second model area for improving sericulture was added in Lin'an, and sericulture improvement areas were established in Wuxing, Jiaxing, Haiyan, Haining, Changxing, Hangzhou, Deqing, Shengxian, Wukang, Zhuji, Yuhang, and other counties to facilitate promotion. In order to unite all sectors to thoroughly improve sericulture, the department also organized the Jiangsu-Zhejiang Sericulture Unified Control Committee with the Jiangsu Department of Construction and leaders of the sericulture industry in the fall of last year to implement a unified policy. The purchase and sale of silkworm seeds, the amount of seed rearing, disinfection, and cocoon collection should all be subject to its control. This is about the improvement aspect. However, the decline of silk industry, the active improvement of the treatment is a radical cure, and the sales of old silk and old cocoons is even more urgent. For this reason, the Department of Construction repeatedly discussed with the Ministry of Industry, the Jiangsu Department of Construction, and the Shanghai financial industry this spring to organize the Jiangsu-Zhejiang Committee for Old Silk and Old Cocoon and the Committee for Promoting the Sales of Old Silk, and tried to promote sales. The National Government issued a short-term public bond of 3 million yuan for the silk industry in Jiangsu and Zhejiang to subsidize exports. In May, it also met with the Department of Finance and the financial industry in Hangzhou to decide that the financial industry would organize the Zhejiang Provincial Silver and Money Industry Joint Committee for Releasing Cocoon Funds to raise 1.8 million yuan in cash for relief. Although all these methods are temporary solutions, they are beneficial to the silk farmers in various counties.

Improving the Cotton Industry 82

According to a survey in 1931, the area planted with cotton in Zhejiang Province totaled 1,981,187 mu, and the annual output of ginned cotton was 519,644 dan. However, the province's total consumption is about 1.1 million dan per year, a shortage of 600,000 dan. In view of this, the Department of Construction specially invited cotton industry experts, representatives from various yarn factories and banks to hold a cotton production meeting in November last year, and ordered the cotton farms and related cotton-producing counties to comply with the resolutions. The Provincial Cotton Farm itself propagated millions of cotton seeds, estimated at 18,820 jin. In addition, more than 60,000 jin were collected from the private sector. After strict selection, about 1,220 jin of good seeds were obtained, which can be promoted to more than 10,000 mu of cotton fields. At the same time, the cotton industry institutions were also improved. The Hangzhou Breeding Farm was changed to the Qibao Breeding Area, expanding the cotton fields to 160 mu, specializing in the cotton production improvement project along the Yangtze River in western Zhejiang. The Xinpu Coastal Branch and the Zhuxiang Branch were both changed to breeding areas, specializing in the cotton industry improvement project along the coast of eastern Zhejiang. In addition, more than 300 mu of new cotton fields were opened in the Toutang area of Xiaoshan to establish the Toutang Breeding Area, which also handles the cotton production improvement project along the Yangtze River in eastern Zhejiang. The original Yuyao, Cixi, Pinghu, Shangyu, Xiaoshan, and other branch farms and breeding areas were changed to cooperative cotton farms, jointly managed with the county governments.

Adjusting Finance 83

The establishment of the Department was due to the increasing bankruptcy of the rural economy. As a plan for reforming the economy, in May of the seventeenth year, it guided the organization of cooperatives and established a training program for cooperative business guidance personnel to cultivate such personnel. There were two phases, totaling seventy-six people. As of the end of June this year, a total of 720 societies had been reported to the Department and approved for registration, with 19,558 members, a total share capital of 89,561 yuan, and a guarantee amount of 124,518 yuan. In order to arouse farmers' interest and belief in cooperative businesses, a rural cooperative business experimental area was established in Qibao, Hangzhou, in March of this year to set up a cooperative model. It is also planned to set up a second rural cooperative business experimental area in Yongjia, which is currently under preparation. Furthermore, in order to regulate farmers' finances, the provincial government allocated 500,000 yuan of capital from the summer of the seventeenth year to the autumn of the eighteenth year as shares in the China Agricultural and Industrial Bank, establishing a branch in Hangzhou, and successively allocating 327,000 yuan of farmer loan funds to lend to various rural cooperatives for agricultural production purposes. As for farmer financial institutions in various counties, those that have established county farmer banks include Jiaxing and six other counties, with a total capital exceeding 400,000 yuan; those that have established farmer lending offices include Jiashan and twenty-one other counties, with a total capital of more than 257,000 yuan; those that have established farmer bank preparatory offices include Wuyi and nine other counties, with a total capital reaching more than 19,000 yuan; and Tonglu is the one county that has established a farmer lending office preparatory office, having raised 5,000 yuan. In total, farmer financial institutions have been established in 37 counties throughout the province, with a total capital reaching more than 682,000 yuan.

Prospecting for Minerals 84

Zhejiang Province is rich in mineral deposits in various counties. The Mineral Products Office under the Department has divided the province into five zones for investigation, collecting various mineral products, specimens, and displaying and testing them separately. It has also organized a drilling team to drill and prospect for geological mineral deposits. The areas that have been investigated include the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway line in the first district in the nineteenth year; the second district from Lanxi to Xiaoshan and from Jiande to Suian in the twentieth year; the Xuanping silver mine, Yiwu coal field, and mineral products in various counties along the Xin'an River basin in the third district from Yongjia via Qingtian, Lishui, Yunhe and other six counties in the twenty-first year. The places that have been drilled successively include the Xucun water source, the coal fields of Jiangshan and Yiwu, the geology of the Haining Tang'an, and the bridge foundation of the Jinhua River Bridge.

Promoting Industry and Commerce 85

Zhejiang Province was originally a prosperous place, but in recent years, internal and external troubles, and the squeeze of civil strife have led to the increasing decline of the rural economy. Not only is it difficult to start new businesses, but even existing businesses are in jeopardy. The authorities are therefore encouraging, protecting, guiding, and assisting, taking into account all aspects. For manufacturers, they promote domestic goods. Since the nineteenth year, they have held domestic goods exhibitions every year. For laborers, they send personnel to inspect factories. If there are any factories that do not comply with the Factory Law, they will be severely punished, and it is stipulated that all factories, companies, shops, etc. that employ 50 to 200 workers must set up labor education or labor classes. Currently, 44 counties and cities have reported the situation of handling labor education to the Department of Construction.

Electrical Businesses 86

The electrical business is of great importance to the development of industry and commerce. After the electrical business in Zhejiang Province was taken over by the government, the Electrical Bureau was established. In the winter of the nineteenth year, the provincial government vigorously implemented austerity measures, and in order to save more than 60,000 yuan in administrative expenses each year, the bureau was abolished. All electrical businesses were handled by the Department of Construction. Later, in order to complete the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway, the authorities entrusted the operation of the four public power plants in Hangzhou, Haining, Yuhang, and Si'an to the Qixin Banking Syndicate with an overdraft limit of 3 million yuan in national currency. The syndicate returned the collateral paid by the former government, totaling 1.9 million yuan in face value of construction bonds, and repaid the principal and interest of the government shares in installments. During the entrustment period, the Department of Construction successively supervised and ordered the Qixin Banking Syndicate in the twenty-first year to complete the equipment of the new Hangzhou power plant and the main line project of the electrical grid. In July of the twenty-first year, the authorities continued to raise funds for the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway, and transferred the entire assets of the plant and its affiliated power plants, as well as the exclusive electrical rights, to the Qixin Banking Syndicate for a price of 6.6 million yuan. After clearing everything, there was still approximately 1 million yuan left. Since these four power plants were transferred to the syndicate, all power plants in the province were privately operated. Currently, there are more than 120 power plants in the province. There is a lack of both capital and talent. The Department of Construction should send personnel to investigate and provide on-site guidance in order to improve them. In the twentieth year, local administrative organs were instructed to strictly pursue users who owed fees, and requests to add small surcharges were rejected. Protection, guidance, and rectification of private power companies are being taken care of in all aspects.

Rectifying the Fisheries Industry 87

Zhejiang Province has a coastline of more than a thousand miles, with rivers crisscrossing the interior, and lakes, ponds, and pools scattered everywhere. The richness of aquatic products is the best in the Southeast. Dinghai originally had a fisheries school and a aquatic product manufacturing factory. In the past three years, in addition to allocating 10,000 yuan to purchase instruments and build aquaculture experimental pools for the fisheries school, the authorities have also hired experts to give lectures, and allocated funds to send students to various fishing vessels for internships and to investigate coastal aquatic products to improve the students' level. The admission qualification has been changed from graduation from elementary school to graduation from junior high school. The study period has been changed from five years to three years, and an aquaculture department has been established. For the aquatic product manufacturing factory, the organization has been improved, a factory director has been appointed, the Minsheng fishing vessel has been transferred to the factory, and another guarantee has been given to raise funds, and 15,000 yuan has been overdrawn from the Dinghai Local Bank for the purpose of collecting fresh and refrigerated products. A total of 16 fishing trips were made in one year, with a catch of 363,732 catties. Up to the end of June in the twenty-second year, 12 fishing trips were made, with a catch of 177,302 catties.

Songjiang: Approving the Widening of Streets 88

Songyi is located at the intersection of Shanghai and Hangzhou, and land and water transportation can be reached in an instant. Since the opening of automobile traffic between Songjiang and Shanghai, people from all over have come to Songjiang to visit in an endless stream. The bridges in the city have gradually been rebuilt and are now passable. However, the roads are still extremely narrow, and cars cannot enter the streets, which is very inconvenient. There was a proposal to widen Changqiao Street, but it has not been implemented due to the difficulty in raising funds. County Magistrate Jin believes that road transportation is a key factor in the appearance of the city, and he believes that it is necessary to widen the streets. Based on the actual measurement of the city's street map by the Technical Office, it was submitted to yesterday's county government meeting for discussion. It was decided to appoint Public Security Bureau Chief Shen Jing, Education Bureau Chief Zhu Zhaosheng, District Chief Zhong Taishi of the First District, and Chief Li Zuhua of the Property Department to conduct a detailed review at the county government at 1:00 p.m. today (the 5th). They all agreed that the old streets in the city were less than three meters wide, and transportation was indeed inconvenient. Based on the map measured by the Technical Office, only the area within the city circle was considered. It was decided to stipulate the widening degree according to the needs of the situation. The main street was set at 12 meters, including the sidewalks, and the secondary ones were divided into 9 meters, 7 meters, and 4 meters. It was noted on the map where to start from which street, and how to raise the funds. The plan will be submitted to the meeting for approval and implementation.

Central Government Sends Personnel to Inquire About Prisoners 89

Yu Qi and Cui Zixin, two members sent by the Central Party Department, came to Songjiang today (the 5th) to pay their respects to the standing committee of the county party department, stating that they were ordered to investigate the situation of political prisoners in prisons in various counties. Tan Baoren, the standing member of the Supervision Committee, accompanied them to the county prison. Prison Officer Su Yan introduced several prisoners and inquired in detail. After the public duty was completed, they left Songjiang on the same day.

Suzhou: A Teenage Boy from Tianjin Attempts Suicide in a Hotel 90

At 4:00 p.m. on the (4th), a teenage boy wearing a dark blue striped serge suit, white serge pants, yellow leather shoes, and a bronze felt hat, carrying a white raincoat on his arm and a leather suitcase in his hand, a copy of the newspaper, and a guest registration card from the Garden Hotel, arrived at the hotel in a horse-drawn carriage. He asked the front desk to pay the carriage fare of four dimes. Then he opened room number 25. He wrote his name on the guest form as Yu Nengrong, a student, 21 years old, from Tianjin. He paid a room fee of three yuan. He then strolled around the garden for a week. At around 5:00 p.m., he ordered half a catty of Huadiao wine, a preserved egg, and a plate of shredded pork for solo drinking. After dinner, he went to bed at around 8:00 p.m. He told the bellboy to wake him up at 8:00 or 9:00 a.m. the next morning. At around 8:00 a.m. yesterday (the 5th), the bellboy opened the door to wake him up, seeing that the time had arrived. He was shocked to see the guest lying on the bed, barely breathing. There was vomit of food next to his head, and three empty bottles and an empty box of Great Britain cigarettes next to the bed, with traces resembling opium. Knowing that the guest had taken poison, he quickly reported to the front desk and sent Yu Nengrong to Suyong Hospital. Dr. Gu examined him and determined that he had swallowed too much opium and tranquilizer, and had delayed for too long. He gave him three injections of cardiac stimulant and gave him an enema. However, his throat was blocked and water could not enter. It was feared that he could not be saved.

New Public Security Bureau Chief Takes Office 91

Shen Gaozhen, the chief of the Third and Second Districts of the Water Public Security Bureau, was commissioned to serve as the chief of the Wuxian Public Security Bureau. Wei Zhanyuan was appointed to fill the vacancy. Wei had already taken over the affairs of the Second District the day before. The Third District will be handed over approximately today or tomorrow. Shen took over the new position as the chief of the Wuxian Public Security Bureau yesterday (the 5th). It is said that the former chief, Mao Naigong, will follow Zhao Qizhou to Ganzhou to take charge of bandit suppression work.

Wujiang: The Trend of Tenant Farmers霸租Will Expand 92

Shen A’kui and Shen A’mao of Xinzizhen, Liudu, Shiqu of Wujiang County, owed Sun Senyu more than 50 shi of rent for more than ten years for more than seven mu of rented land. They returned the land last winter, but the rent was not paid in full. As a result, Sun Senyu filed a civil lawsuit in February, but the defendants ignored it and intensified their efforts. When the plaintiff hired workers to pump water to prepare for transplanting rice seedlings, they aggressively went to the field to prevent the plaintiff's workers from entering the field. Fearing that there would be trouble, they tried their best to avoid it. Unexpectedly, A’kui and others thought they could be bullied and planted the cultivated land without permission. Sun Senyu had no other choice but to file a criminal lawsuit again. Who knew that A’kui and others still ignored it, causing the case to be suspended for eight months without resolution. Therefore, A’kui and others regarded 霸租and rent arrears as their due right. They boasted to the tenants in the neighboring zhen that the government now does not protect the owners, and everyone can not pay the rent. Even if they are sued, it is nothing more than that. They hoped to mobilize the tenants to follow suit and support them. Those who heard it envied their benefits and were all excited. Therefore, there will inevitably be problems with the rents in the zhen now. However, the authorities have heard about it, and I don't know if they can eliminate the hidden dangers.

Changzhou: The Hangyou Boat from Jiangyin Robbed Again 93

The Hangyou boat sailing from Wuyi to Qingyizhen, Jiangyin, was robbed a few days ago, and the losses were huge. The county government is ordering the police to strictly arrest the robbers. Unexpectedly, on the evening of the 3rd, the Hangyou boat sailing from Changzhou to Jiangyin was passing through the Xilongtan area near Yantou Bridge, and four bandits suddenly jumped out of the field, each holding a Brownie pistol. One person was on the bow acting as a lookout, and two people entered the cabin to search and rob. All the goods on the boat and the passengers' silver were completely robbed. Yesterday (the 4th), the victim reported the case to the county government. The county government ordered the Hangyou Boat Association to instruct all Hangyou boats to prohibit sailing at night to avoid danger, as the Hangyou boats have been robbed repeatedly at night. At the same time, it also ordered the police to strictly arrest the robbers in this case and bring them to justice.

Nantong: Refugees Robbed Sianzhen 94

Four hundred refugees from Hebei Province arrived in Nantong's Sianzhen on the evening of the 3rd. Because their demand for food and supplies was not met, they suddenly robbed all the shops and residents in the zhen. The Qian Changqia and other families suffered the greatest losses. The police and militia immediately went to suppress the robbery and captured eight ringleaders, including Chen Jinkun, and sent them to the county government. The remaining refugees were escorted out of the territory.

Coastal Counties Surveyed and Constructed Shooting Ranges 95

The county magistrates of Nantong, Haimen, Rugao, and Qidong, all coastal counties, were ordered by the Military Commission to survey and construct suitable shooting ranges with a length of 300 meters. The Nantong County Government has surveyed and determined the target range next to Jianshan Xianshandong and will build it for use in the near future.

The Seventh District Commissioner Takes Office 96

The newly appointed Administrative Inspector of the Seventh District, Cheng Yuqi, arrived in Tongzhou from Shanghai on the 4th. At noon, he took over the seal of the commissioner and county magistrate of Nantong, and announced the appointment of the staff: Yu Guoguang as the secretary of the commissioner's office, Zhong Mengling as the secretary of the county government, Yu Fumin as the chief of the First Section, and Long Jun as the chief of the Second Section.

Jiangyin: The Sheng Family Estate is Ordered to be Returned by the Province 97

The Sheng family estate of Jimeijunda, the county, was previously seized by the province. It was previously ordered to lift the seizure. The provincial government believes that the case has been pending for many years and is of great importance. It should be investigated separately before handling. It was previously resolved by the Provincial Government Committee in the 599th meeting. According to the report submitted by Sheng Enyi and others, 60,000 yuan was allocated from the return of private property for construction expenses. The request was approved, and the counties were ordered to return the estate. County Magistrate Ruan has followed the order after receiving it.

Xiaoshan: A Couple Commits Suicide Due to Illness and Poverty 98

Guo Rongsheng, a resident of Yintou, outside the east gate of Xiaoshan, used to be a mechanic. He returned home from Hangzhou last month due to illness. He repeatedly consulted doctors and took medicine, but did not fully recover. By the Mid-Autumn Festival, he was heavily in debt and had no way to solve it. On the 3rd, his wife, Chen, went to her relatives' house to borrow money, but did not get a penny. She reported to her husband. Guo, overwhelmed by illness and poverty, had no way to survive, so he hanged himself at midnight on the same day and died. The next morning, his wife, Chen, said that her husband had committed suicide due to debt, and also threw herself into the pond behind the house and died. Only two daughters, aged three and seven, were left in the family, in a very miserable state.

Huzhou: The Huxin Night Boat Was Robbed 99

The night boat from Xinshi to Huzhou departed from Xinshi on the afternoon of the 1st of this month. When it passed through the Lucun Port entrance near Yuanjiahui, it suddenly encountered a boat shaped like a yellow duck boat. There were several bandits inside, holding wooden-shell guns, who ordered the boat to stop. The bandits immediately boarded the boat and robbed it, stealing five pieces of Jinde Shun silk, two pieces of clothing material, six pieces of cotton cloth, six catties of Chen Yuangan silk thread, and more than thirty yuan in cash.

Jiaxing: A Member of the Militia Shot Himself 100

Yu Fusong, a member of the Jiaxing Lengyan Temple-based County Security Regiment's cadre team, was a native of Chongde County, 25 years old. He was recommended by the Seventh District and enrolled in the regiment. Yu was usually taciturn and extremely disciplined, but he occasionally showed a lack of interest in life to the other members of the regiment, which no one paid attention to. The 4th was the ancient Mid-Autumn Festival. Yu bought cigarettes and distributed them to the other members of the regiment, and then bought food from the restaurant and ate a lot. At about 6:00 p.m., Yu replaced Wu Zhenji, who was on guard duty at the gate, and ordered Wu to have dinner. Unexpectedly, in less than five minutes, Yu shot himself with his gun, the bullet piercing his chest. Hengshan, a monk from the temple, heard the sound and came out to look. Yu had already fallen to the ground. The regiment immediately carried Yu to the Gospel Hospital for treatment, but he died due to his serious injuries. He was then carried back to the regiment. At 3:00 p.m. on the 5th, Wang Bangyan, the prosecutor of the local branch court, went to the Lengyan Temple team headquarters to examine the body. It was confirmed that he had shot himself with his gun, so he immediately prepared a coffin for the funeral.

Local Bank Issues Exchange Vouchers 101

The Jiaxing Branch of the Zhejiang Provincial Local Bank has received a large number of exchange vouchers from the head office and issued them yesterday. There are three types of vouchers: one yuan, five yuan, and ten yuan. There are also two types of auxiliary currency vouchers: ten cents and twenty cents. Most of the shops in the city have already used them. The bank has made full preparations to redeem them at any time, and the county chamber of commerce has notified all shops to circulate and use them.

Because the Ministry of Finance urgently needed to discuss the issuance of 100 million yuan of new customs treasury bonds with the banking community in Shanghai, Song flew from Beijing to Shanghai by private plane at 8:30 yesterday morning, accompanied by Dr. Leith-Ross, Tang Hai'an, and Leith-Ross's secretary, Max, totaling four people. Large-Scale Reproduction of Rare Books; Peking Library and Commercial Press Drafted a Contract 104

The Ministry of Education ordered the Peking Library in July to prepare for the reproduction of rare books to promote our country's inherent culture. The library immediately contacted major libraries and book collectors in the country, all of whom expressed their full support because it was a matter of promoting academics. The library and the Commercial Press drafted a contract. Now we have found the library's submission to the Ministry of Education with two sets of measures and thirteen articles of the contract, which are extremely important, so we transcribe them as follows:

Submission 105

The director of the Peking Library submitted to the Ministry of Education, stating that the Ministry sent a letter on July 19th commissioning the library to be responsible for preparing for the printing of rare books. A plan was drafted and reported to the Ministry for record. The Ministry's intention to promote culture and benefit scholars is greatly appreciated. The library immediately repeatedly reviewed and protected the plan with public and private collectors and the Commercial Press, and drafted two sets of measures, which are now recorded on separate paper and submitted for review, along with a volume of the proposed catalog of Siku Rare Book Series (other existing catalogs and uncollected proposed catalogs will be submitted after compilation). A draft contract between the library and the Commercial Press is submitted for review and record, which is for the public convenience. Respectfully submitted to the Minister of Education, with one copy of the proposed catalog, one copy of the draft contract, and one copy of the measures. Cai Yuanpei, Director of the National Peking Library, Yuan Tongli, Deputy Director (September 25th)

Measures 106

Two sets of measures are attached: (1) The books selected for the Rare Book Series are not limited to those recorded in the Siku Quanshu. Generally speaking, they can be divided into three categories: (A) Old carvings and old transcriptions that are better than the Siku editions; (B) Those that were not included when compiling the Siku Quanshu; (C) Those recorded in the Siku existing catalogs. The editions not found when compiling the Siku have been emerging one after another in the past few decades. In addition to the Peking Library and the National Studies Library, collectors at home and abroad, such as Qu Qijia of Changshu, Li Shengduo of Dehua, Chuan Zengxiang of Jiang'an, Liu Chenggan of Wuxing, Pan Mingxun of Panyu, and Mo Tianyi of Dongguan, are all worthy of being called outstanding for a generation. In addition, there are countless lost books from Dunhuang and Japan, which should be investigated separately and reproduced in the best condition. In addition, the books recorded in the Siku existing catalogs, as well as the Ming Shilu, and the banned books during the Qianlong period of the Qing Dynasty, which were all discarded due to taboos when compiling the Siku, should also be published separately to supplement the omissions of the official history and satisfy the scholars' wishes. It is planned to first publish the books of category A, and then gradually extend to categories B and C, to show the Ministry's intention to promote culture. (2) The aim of reproducing the books is to circulate them. Each book should be sold at a low price as a separate edition after printing, and then combined into a series, so that each book is a separate book, so that poor scholars can easily purchase them, and the rare books can be widely spread, so as not to betray the Ministry's original intention of promoting academics and benefiting scholars.

Contract 107

The Peiping Library and the Commercial Press Draw Up a Contract: The National Peiping Library (hereinafter referred to as Party A) and the Shanghai Commercial Press (hereinafter referred to as Party B), with the mutual agreement to have Party A's rare books reproduced and published, hereby enter into the following conditions: Article 1: Party A entrusts Party B with the reproduction and subsequent publication of its collection of rare books. Article 2: The selection of rare books in the preceding article shall be determined through consultation between both parties. However, if after selection, technical issues prevent photography, or if the photographs are unclear, only those items may be excluded from printing. Article 3: For all books decided to be printed, Party A shall be responsible for writing an afterword or collation notes, which Party A shall provide to Party B before printing. Article 4: All books shall be reduced to a small size similar to the "Siku Congkan." The number of copies printed and the retail price shall be determined by Party B. Any books that can be reproduced in their original format without using the small size shall also be determined through consultation between both parties. Article 5: All books shall use handmade Lian Shi paper or Mao Bian paper. Article 6: Selected books shall be transported by Party A to Shanghai and handed over to Party B. Upon receipt, Party B shall issue a receipt (clearly stating the edition, number of volumes, number of scrolls, and number of pages) to Party A for its record. Party B shall also carefully preserve the received books and prevent any damage. After the photography is completed, the books shall be returned to Party A. Upon receipt by Party A, the aforementioned receipt shall be returned to Party B. Article 7: The transportation costs from Peiping to Shanghai shall be borne by Party A, and all costs for transportation back from Shanghai shall be borne by Party B. Article 8: For the photography and printing, Party B shall provide Party A with one-tenth of the actual number of copies printed, solely for the purpose of gifting to libraries in various provinces and cities and for international exchange. Article 9: The effective period of this contract is temporarily set at three years. Upon expiration, both parties may agree to renew or revise it. Article 10: If the contract is not continued upon expiration, Party B shall still compensate Party A according to the provisions of Article 8 when publishing books that have already been photographed. Article 11: During and after the term of this contract, Party A agrees not to lend the books already photographed by Party B to others or reproduce them itself. Article 12: This contract is made in duplicate, with each party holding one copy as proof. It shall come into effect after being filed with the Ministry of Education. Article 13: For rare books held by national, public, or private entities that Party A introduces to Party B for separate contract negotiation, reproduction, and publication, the format should, to the extent possible, follow the provisions of this contract. Contract established on the ____ day of the ____ month of the 22nd year of the Republic of China. National Peiping Library, Shanghai Commercial Press.

Mr. Ariyoshi Akira is scheduled to go to the capital within days, and will travel via Peiping. According to what he knows, the Japanese ambassador's trip is purely for inspecting embassy affairs and socializing with the mission, and there are no special tasks, it is said. The New Voice News agency said that the news that Japan will use reciprocal tariffs as an exchange condition and is willing to automatically revoke consular jurisdiction in China has attracted the attention of those who are quite concerned about international issues. A reporter from the New Voice News Agency made a special trip to visit Mr. Zhuang Zuobin, our country's ambassador to Japan, last night to inquire about everything. Mr. Zhuang expressed that he only saw it in the newspaper, and nothing has been heard from official channels, and that it is a mistranslation of the Japanese telegram and not the opinion of the Japanese diplomatic authorities, and so on.

Three Types of Government Bonds; Principal Repaid by Lottery This Morning; Total of Six Tranches Drawn, Repaying Principal of 840,000 Yuan; Silk Industry and Finance to Pay Instalments on the 15th, Demobilization at the End of the Month 109

The seventh principal repayment of the Short-Term Financial Government Bonds of the 20th Year of the Republic of China, the thirteenth principal repayment of the Demobilization Government Bonds of the 18th Year of the Republic of China, and the third principal repayment of the Jiangsu-Zhejiang Silk Industry Government Bonds of the 20th Year of the Republic of China were all held at 10:00 AM this morning at the auditorium of the Banking Association at No. 4 Hong Kong Road. A total of 840,000 yuan was repaid in principal. The silk industry and finance will start paying the installments from the 15th of this month by the Central Bank and other banks. Demobilization will be at the end of this month. The details are recorded as follows:

Representatives Present 110

The following supervisors and auditors were present: Wang Qizhi from the Auditing Department; Guo Weibai from the Industry Department; Yu Zuoting from the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce; Fan Jietang from the Foundation Management Committee; Tang Shoumin from the Shanghai Banking Association; Qian Yuansheng from the Shanghai Money Shop Association; Li Tisheng from the Central Bank (lottery drawer); Zhu Qizhen from the Bank of China; Mao Rui from the Bank of Communications; Huang Guoen (manager); Dong Puming; He Xiaojuan; Liang Yaozong; Chen Shaochao (registrar); You Dundi; Ji Juncai; Huang Qizong (document clerk); Ling Qixun; Xu Zuhuang; Huang Meizhao; Zheng Yijian (greeter); Chen Jian; Xia Jilin from the Hankou Chamber of Commerce; Song Ziliang from the National Goods Bank; Chen Gan-I from the Jiangsu-Zhejiang Silk Industry Government Bonds Custody Committee; Ju Zhijing from the First Special District Court; Dong Xuntian from the Peiping Chamber of Commerce; Zhu Qizhen from the Tianjin Chamber of Commerce; Luo Quyuan from the Chinese Securities Exchange; and more than forty others.

Chairman's Report 111

Zheng Lai, Director of the Government Bonds Department, reported: "Today is the day for the seventh principal repayment lottery of the Short-Term Financial Government Bonds of the 20th Year of the Republic of China, the third principal repayment lottery of the Jiangsu-Zhejiang Silk Industry Government Bonds of the 20th Year of the Republic of China, and the thirteenth principal repayment of the Demobilization Government Bonds of the 18th Year of the Republic of China. I am extremely pleased that you have all come to attend. The total amount of the Short-Term Financial Government Bonds of the 20th Year of the Republic of China issued was 80 million yuan. In addition to the first to sixth repayments, which have already been drawn, this time is the seventh repayment, with two tranches drawn, each tranche being 80,000 yuan, totaling 160,000 yuan, which is 2/1000 of the total amount of government bonds issued. Therefore, the lottery method is to use bonds with the same last three digits as the winning bonds. The actual amount of the Jiangsu-Zhejiang Silk Industry Government Bonds of the 20th Year of the Republic of China issued was 6 million yuan. In addition to the first and second repayments, which have already been drawn, this time is the third repayment, with three tranches drawn, totaling 180,000 yuan, which is 3% of the actual amount of bonds issued. Therefore, the lottery method is to use bonds with the same last two digits as the winning bonds. The total amount of the Demobilization Government Bonds of the 18th Year of the Republic of China issued was 50 million yuan. In addition to the first and second repayments, which have already been drawn, this time is the thirteenth repayment, with one tranche drawn, totaling 500,000 yuan, which is 1% of the total amount of government bonds issued. Therefore, the lottery method is also to use bonds with the same last two digits as the winning bonds. The aforementioned three types of winning bonds, the Short-Term Financial Government Bonds of the 20th Year of the Republic of China, and the Jiangsu-Zhejiang Silk Industry Government Bonds of the 20th Year of the Republic of China, are scheduled to be paid from the 15th of this month, and the Demobilization Government Bonds of the 18th Year of the Republic of China are scheduled to be paid from the 31st of this month. Except for the Silk Industry Government Bonds, which are paid by the Central Bank, the Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, and the National Goods Bank, the rest are still paid by the Central Bank, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications, along with the interest due, all paid in national currency, regardless of location. Please have the supervisors check the lottery slips and the slip books so that the lottery can be executed."

Winning Numbers 112

After the Chairman's report, the supervisors checked the lottery slips and the slip books, followed by the execution by the lottery drawers. All drawn numbers were announced and recorded on a sign, and the supervisors stamped the slip books. As for the winning numbers: (1) Two tranches of Short-Term Financial Government Bonds: [No. 014], [No. 697]; (2) Three tranches of Zhejiang Silk Industry Government Bonds: [No. 26], [No. 31], [No. 76]; (3) One tranche of Demobilization Government Bonds: [No. 26]; totaling 840,000 yuan in principal repayment.

Statistics team: Jin Houcheng. The rest is omitted. The meeting adjourned.

Charter Approved 122

Jiangsu Chuan-Nan Bao-Qi Flood Relief Association Charter. (Article 1) The purpose of this association is to provide relief to the victims of the flood in the five counties of Chuansha, Nanhui, Chongming, Baoshan, and Qidong. (Article 2) This association is jointly initiated and organized by charitable and public welfare organizations and individuals in Shanghai. Anyone who supports the purpose of this association, regardless of province, city, nationality, or gender, may join the association as a member. (Article 3) The association's office is located at the Renji Shantang on Yunnan Road in Shanghai, with a branch office at No. 270 Sichuan Road. (Article 4) This association raises relief funds and goods and directly handles disaster relief matters in the disaster area in accordance with the methods of charitable relief. (Article 5) This association has one chairman, five vice-chairmen, one honorary chairman, a number of executive committee members, and a number of supervisory committee members, who are publicly nominated from among the members. The chairman may nominate one of the vice-chairmen to reside in the association and take charge of all affairs. Twenty-five members are publicly nominated from among the executive committee members to serve as standing committee members. (Article 6) The executive committee of this association has the following eight teams: general affairs team, fundraising team, finance team, investigation and distribution team, sanitation team, statistics team, procurement team, and transportation team. The supervisory committee of this association has the following two teams: audit team and inspection team. The detailed rules for each team will be formulated separately. (Article 7) Each team of this association may have a director and a deputy director, who are nominated by the chairman and approved by the general meeting or the joint meeting of the executive and supervisory committees. (Article 8) The standing committee of this association meets once a week, and the joint meeting of the executive and supervisory committees meets once a month. The chairman and vice-chairmen all attend the meetings. If there are important matters, a temporary meeting may be held, which is convened by the chairman. However, if five or more executive or supervisory committee members agree, they may also request the chairman to convene a meeting. (Article 9) The relief funds and goods received by this association are handled by this association and the designated bank. (Article 10) The relief funds and goods received by this association are allocated by this association, unless the donor specifies the use. Those sent directly to the disaster area should be reported to this association by the office in that county every 1st and 16th of the month. (Article 11) This association establishes separate detailed procedures for receiving and sending relief funds and goods. All service personnel must abide by them. The status of receipts and disbursements will be announced in the newspaper at any time and a statement of accounts, which has been audited by the accountant, is published at the end. (Article 12) In the event of an emergency, the relevant team may consult with the chairman and jointly be responsible for handling it. It will be submitted to the next executive and supervisory committee meeting or general meeting for ratification. (Article 13) Each county establishes an office. The organization may be increased or decreased as appropriate according to local conditions, but it shall not conflict with the purpose and principles of this association. (Article 14) This charter shall be implemented after being approved by the general meeting. If there are any shortcomings that need to be amended, they shall also be decided by the general meeting and approved.

The Speed of Wireless Radio: Marconi Sends a Signal from the Chicago World's Fair 129

The Shanghai Times reports that on Tuesday of this week, the Chicago World's Fair, celebrating "Marconi Day," invited wireless radio inventor Marconi to a banquet that evening. During the banquet, Marconi sent a wireless "SSS" signal, which was transmitted through six major radio stations around the world. First, it went to New York, then to Rome, then to Berlin, then to Manila, then to Shanghai, then to San Francisco, and finally back to Chicago via New York. The message circled the globe in thirty-three seconds, according to news from Chicago yesterday. This demonstrates the astonishing speed of wireless radio.

Methods for Revising Pawnshop License Fees: Two Per Thousand for Large Pawnshops, Four Per Thousand for Small Pawnshops 130

An announcement released by the Public Works Department states that, for the past three years, the license fees for pawnshops in the Public Settlement have been changed to a fixed annual amount based on the size of the establishment. The pawnshop industry raised objections to this. Recently, the Finance Committee of the Public Works Department considered the matter and the Finance Department proposed a revised method: fees would still be collected based on each shop's annual turnover. The calculation method would use the annual turnover for the twelve months up to the end of September as the standard for the following year's tax payment (January to December). Payments would still be collected in four quarterly installments. After discussion, one committee member stated that large pawnshops and small pawnshops operate completely differently and each has its own guild. For example, large pawnshops generally do not charge storage fees except for extremely large items, while small pawnshops charge storage and other fees even for small items like jewelry. It was then resolved that the Director of Finance should consult with the pawnshop guilds to reduce the current license fees to two per thousand of annual turnover for large pawnshops and four per thousand for small pawnshops, effective January 1, 1934. This proposal was approved by the Board of Directors on October 3 and will be implemented accordingly.

Two Groups Petition the Court to Severely Punish Unscrupulous Merchants in the Case of Japanese Yarn Passed off as Domestic Goods; Request that They Be Charged with Forgery of Official Documents and Fraud 131

The Hua Dong News Agency reports that the sensational case of ten factories, including Gong Zu and Ding Xin, privately selling enemy goods, passing off Ren Zhong brand domestic yarn from Shen Xin No. 5 Factory, and forging tax invoices to deceive the tax authorities for shipping purposes, is scheduled for continued trial today. However, since Shen Xin and Gong Zu, Ding Xin, etc., have reached a settlement, today's hearing may be resolved immediately. Therefore, He Zicheng, Executive Committee Member of the Zhijiang Shipping Guild of Hangzhou, and Li Qiaozhi, Executive Committee Member of the United Associations of Various People's Groups in Shanghai, out of patriotic fervor, yesterday requested lawyer Zhang Juansheng to draft a petition to the First Special District Court, criminally charging the unscrupulous merchants Yu Xifan, Chen Zhongxian, Wang Liwei, Sun Xinzu, Yu Yuxin, Zhou Songmao, Chai Zhixiang, Zhao Bingnan, Wang Gengsheng, Guan Bingqing, etc., with the crimes of forging official documents and fraud, in order to prevent wrongdoing and uphold national law. The petition states: "Regarding the matter of using fraudulent methods and forging official documents to harm public and private interests, we request strict punishment according to law. The ten factories, including Gong Zu Sock Factory, used the tax certificate of the Da Kang Yarn Factory's 'Standing Horse' brand of Japanese merchants to forge it into Ren Zhong brand of Shen Xin and other five factories, and also forged the consolidated tax certificate of the Jiangsu-Zhejiang-Anhui Tax Bureau. This was discovered by the Tax Bureau, which notified Shen Xin No. 5 Factory. The factory then filed a private prosecution. Your court has already held a hearing and set a deadline for retrial. The aforementioned circumstances have been publicly tried and reported, causing widespread consternation. Since the September 18th Incident, when the violent Japanese invaded Northeast China, all our countrymen have hated the brutality and ferocity of the island nation, and without exception, have shared the same hatred and determination to save the country. We have unanimously boycotted enemy goods and adhered to passive resistance, hoping to stem the tide. At this time of national crisis and unrecovered territory, all compatriots should embrace the fervent spirit of boycotting Japanese goods. However, the unscrupulous merchants, Gong Zu Sock Factory and other ten factories, are so deranged and recklessly risked disgrace by daring to use the means of forging official documents to commit fraud in an attempt to gain illegal profits. Although only Shen Xin No. 1 Factory is directly harmed, those who are indirectly harmed without knowing it are deeply and greatly affected. Such corrupt, vile, and deceitful merchants who cheat the people of the country cause all those with blood to be outraged. We look forward to the national law punishing them. We deeply grieve the arrogance of the powerful enemy and worry for the country. We have held anti-Japanese posts in Shanghai and Hangzhou. We have no way to completely eliminate these unscrupulous merchants who cheat and seek profit in order to save the country and alleviate the difficulties. Now, fortunately, we have witnessed a large number of incorrigible unscrupulous merchants being uncovered, and their clearly criminal acts with conclusive evidence can be placed under national law and punished with appropriate penalties to deter wrongdoing and warn others. Recently, we have repeatedly read reports that Shen Xin No. 5 Factory has accepted a settlement regarding the damage caused by counterfeiting and is said to be completely withdrawing [the case]. We cannot help but feel great regret. If the outcome of the trial is as reported, it will not only encourage others to follow suit and open the door to counterfeiting and fraud but also disregard the credibility of national law. Out of patriotic fervor, how can we continue to tolerate such a situation and allow [these merchants] to go unpunished outside the law? Therefore, we specially request your court to separately detain the defendants for the forgery of official documents and fraud, and severely punish them according to law, in order to prevent wrongdoing and uphold national law for the benefit of both public and private interests. Respectfully submitted to the First Special District Court of Shanghai."

Appeal of Assassin of Zhao Tieqiao Rejected 142

The assassins Xia Shaoen and Wang Yinshan, who assassinated Zhao Tieqiao, the former Director of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, appealed to the Supreme Court against the Jiangsu High Court's second instance verdict of life imprisonment. —Strange Name Cards and Addresses of Important People Found on His Person—

Liu Shuiling, a native of Pudong, 31 years old, was a leather wallet worker at the Xinhau Leather Factory owned by the Chai brothers, Xinpu and Shunpu, from Ningbo in Furun Lane, Nanshi, Jiujiudi. Liu took advantage of the Mid-Autumn Festival holiday the day before yesterday to visit a friend at Xiaonanmen in the evening. He failed to transfer to the No. 3 loop tram, which led to a dispute when the ticket inspector discovered it. Liu was detained at the Second District General Station. After District Chief Li questioned him, his answers were vague. At the same time, four red-bottomed, gold-lettered name cards were found on his person, printed with [Jiang Jieyan] [Ge Gang] with the inscription "Jiangsu Province, Songjiang Prefecture, Nanhui County, Liuzao Township." Two of them had red name chops. There were also two red paper, gold letter cards printed with [Your Excellency Jieshi], [Jiang Ge Gang], [Jieyan] "Jiangsu Nanhui Heaven-Sent Zhuangyuan, Seven-Province Inspector Censor." On the back were white printed characters meaning "Zhuangyuan and Younger Brother". A total of five strange name cards were found, which contained the addresses of important Party-state figures, such as: (1) [Zhongzheng, 1543 Maojia Lane, Zhongshan East Road, Nanjing; Lishi Society, Central Park, Nanjing; 3655 Gangshan Hot Springs Road, South Gate, Nanjing; 1367 Lane 147, Wutong Village, Zhajiayuan, Hangzhou], (2) [Feng Yuxiang, Zi Huanzhang, Taian County, Shandong; Yongping and others in Mount Tai], (3) [Yan Xishan, Zi Bochuan, 167 Duck Village in Taiyuan City, Shanxi], (4) [Chen Mingshu, 75 Shanzhong Road, French Concession, near Haig Road]. The strange cards were presented as evidence. At the same time, Liu made absurd claims, saying that he had recognized Soong Mei-ling as his stepmother in June of the 19th year of the Republic of China, met her at the Popular Cinema in Nanshi, and was introduced in a dream by Nantze Lu Bohong. District Chief Li, seeing that his words were incoherent, ordered him to be temporarily detained for investigation. It was also learned that in November of last year, Liu had also been found with similar strange cards in Nanjing by the Capital Public Security Bureau. They had ordered the provincial government to instruct the Water Police Team to go to Liuzao Township, Nanhui, for investigation. However, there had been no incidents of external fraud, proving that he suffered from mental illness, and he was released.

Home Broken, Police Officer Saddened, Suicide - Mid-Autumn Festival, Heartsick - After Shift, Gun Suicide 152

Wang Gang, a fourth-class police officer of the Yinhang Branch of the Seventh District of the Jiangwan District Public Security Bureau, was 25 years old, from Hebei Province, and had only been a police officer for three months. On the 4th of this month, the Mid-Autumn Festival according to the old lunar calendar, the beautiful scenery and good festival made him even more homesick. Therefore, Wang was heartbroken. At 12:00 noon, after his shift at the gate, he took the rifle he was carrying to the toilet, aimed it at his head, and fired with a loud bang, falling to the ground and dying. Shen Yangchun - Missing After Being Kidnapped - Kidnapper Gu Junshan Interrogated Yesterday - Gu Junshan Said He Was a Wang Detective's Orderly - Investigation by the French Concession Police Found No Such Person 153

At 10:00 AM yesterday, Judge Li Changnian continued the trial in the First Criminal Court. First, the police lawyer Yuan Huang stated the police investigation process, saying that according to the defendant Gu Junshan's confession, he is currently serving as an orderly at Commander Wang's place in the Headquarters. He came to Shanghai with Wang on the 8th of last month and resided in the Longhua Gendarmerie Camp. On the 16th, he was ordered by Wang to go to the intersection of Route Bubergh in the French Concession at 8:00 AM the next morning with his colleague Wang Junsheng and others to arrest a Communist leader. Someone else was waiting there to point them out. The police sent personnel to the Longhua Headquarters to investigate, but there was no such person as Wang Detective, and the people in the Headquarters did not know the defendant's name. The plaintiff Zhao Liansheng did not arrive.
