The defendant Gu Junshan, 27 years old, from Funing, confessed that he came to Shanghai in December of last year, lived near Longhua with a person surnamed Zhou, pulling a rickshaw for a living. At the beginning of April of this year, he joined the army in the Sixth Platoon, Third Company, First Battalion, Eighty-Eighth Division in Longhua. After a month, he went to Nanjing and stayed for about two months. His fellow villager Zhou Jinsheng recommended him to work as an orderly at Wang Detective's place, with a monthly salary of 16 yuan. After a few days of work, he followed Wang and nine colleagues to Yangzhou for about half a month, where they arrested a Communist. Zhou and another colleague escorted him to Beijing. He and Wang and others returned to Shanghai, eight people in total, and stayed in the Longhua Gendarmerie Camp. Wang lived in a bungalow next to a tea house across from the barracks. On the evening of September 16, at 7:00 PM, Wang called him and his colleague Wang Junsheng to the office and said to them, "Tomorrow morning at 8:00 AM, you two go to the intersection of Route Bubergh and Rue Lubin to arrest a Communist leader." He replied that he did not know him and how could he arrest him. Wang said that another detective familiar with Wang Junsheng would be waiting there to point them out. The next morning, Wang issued each of them a live ammunition pistol in the office and they took a car to the intersection of Rue Lubin and Route Delfosse, got out of the car, and walked to the intersection of Route Bubergh. At about 8:00 AM, Wang Junsheng pointed at a person and said, "That's him." The detective ordered me to wait in the northeast corner. Not long after, I saw two men, a woman, and a child walking out of Bubergh Lane. Wang Junsheng waved to me to help him capture them. One of the two men was the Communist leader that the detective said he was. Just as I was about to step forward, I don't know why Wang Junsheng suddenly fired two shots and captured one person into the car and drove away. When I heard the gunshots, I ran east along Route Bubergh and was arrested by the patrol police. I don't know what happened afterwards. If we could have captured the Communist and not been arrested by the police, we would have escorted him to Wang Detective's place in Longhua, etc. At this point in the interrogation, the court, because the plaintiff Zhao Liansheng had not arrived, announced a postponement and ordered the plaintiff to be summoned for further interrogation. The defendant was still remanded in custody.

Ten Thousand People Vie to See the Zhejiang Tide 154

Car to……Babao

Train to……Haining

Babao The time flies quickly, and it's time to watch the tide again. However, most people only know to gather in Haining, and few know to go to Babao to watch the tide. Babao is more than ten miles east of Haining, and it is indeed an excellent place to watch the tide. Twenty miles east of Babao, the riverbank suddenly becomes towering, and the raging waves rush in and are suddenly counterattacked, dividing into two. The one that is blocked is called the East Tide, and the one that is not blocked is called the South Tide. The two tides surge westward and converge at Babao, then swirl and surge, forming a curved shape before rushing to Haining. Therefore, the tide of Haining is actually the tail of Babao. The China Travel Service, in view of this, has specially organized a Babao Tide Watching Tour this year, and the company has set up a very comfortable enclosure on the seawall there. Take a car from Shanghai along the Haihang Highway directly to Babao. There will be special cars for three days, and you can return to Shanghai that night. It was originally scheduled to start yesterday (5th), but because it happened to be the day after the Mid-Autumn Festival according to the old lunar calendar, people from all walks of life were busy with affairs, so they asked the company to postpone it until today. Yesterday, many people booked tickets, and the continuous driving will continue until Sunday.

Haining The Haining Tide Watching Special Train of the Beijing-Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration is scheduled to start today. It departs from Shanghai North Station. After the car arrives at Xieqiao, it will be transferred to a civilian boat and towed by a ship. A viewing platform will be built next to the Haining seawall, and you can return to Shanghai on the same day. On the 6th, it will depart from Shanghai at 6:50 AM, on the 7th, it will depart from Shanghai at 7:10 AM, and on the 8th, it will depart from Shanghai at 7:45 AM. According to those who are familiar with the Haining tide, this year's tide will be large, especially when the weather is cloudy and rainy. On the 6th, the tide will rise at 12:40 PM, on the 7th, the tide will rise at 1:00 PM, and on the 8th, the tide will rise at 1:30 PM.

The Dagong News Agency reported that the Shanghai Electric Power Company labor strike had the following news yesterday:

Foremen Left the Factory Yesterday Morning 160

Since the workers of both the new and old factories declared a total work slowdown and were refused entry to the factory by the factory, the foremen of the new factory also left the factory voluntarily. Yesterday, all fifty foremen and one hundred temporary workers, according to the decision of the foremen's meeting the day before, joined the work slowdown, so the Chinese workers of the Electric Power Company, except for the power generation workers, have completely slowed down, and the situation is becoming more serious.

Strict Order to Maintain Power Generation 161

The Shanghai General Labor Union yesterday ordered the Fourth District Water and Electricity Labor Union, saying, "In order to comply with the order, since all members of the union have been slowing down due to the unreasonable oppression of the Electric Power Company, they are still considerate of social tranquility and maintain power generation, which is commendable. Recently, the union reported that three shifts of workers (i.e., power generation workers) have repeatedly requested to leave the factory and join the work slowdown, and the union has been unable to stop them. The power generation workers have been suffering deeply and have decided to take unified action. However, once the power is cut off, the society will inevitably suffer a huge panic. If this leads to other changes, although it is caused by the company's oppression, it will have too great an impact on the local area. In addition to already telegraphing the central and municipal party and government authorities to quickly find a way to deal with and resolve the matter as soon as possible, we hereby strictly order the union to immediately relay to the power generation workers to explain the greater good, and not to stop power generation unless absolutely necessary, in order to maintain social order, which is of utmost importance. This order is urgent."

Company Notice to Employees 162

The Shanghai Electric Power Company printed a notice to employees, which was distributed to various employees yesterday. The following is an excerpt of the translation: "Regarding the recent labor dispute at the new and old factories, the news in the Shanghai newspapers said that the Public Works Bureau previously stipulated a 5% pension, which was quite favorable, but now it is thought to be 1% or 2%, which is not accurate. The pension stipulated by the former Public Works Bureau required 20 years of service to be eligible for payment. The current revision by the company stipulates that 15 years or less is eligible for payment, so the method is more favorable than before. However, those who are entrusted with passing or dismissed for cause are not subject to this rule. The three workers who were recently dismissed all committed offenses, and the workers unreasonably requested payment of pensions. The company is unable to accept it. Therefore, the company is not affected by the workers' strike. It is actually the workers who are cutting themselves off from the company. It is hoped that all employees will make a fair judgment and not take any action." Signed, Vice Chairman and Manager Shelt, October 5, 1933.

After the company issued the notice to employees, the Dagong News Agency reporter, in order to understand the attitude of the employees, specially visited the person in charge of the Employees' Union, who said, "Today, the employees have received the company's written letter, the content of which is completely disguised, in an attempt to anesthetize people's hearts. Nowadays, the company dismisses workers at every turn and uses the excuse of having made mistakes to evade pensions. The treatment of Chinese employees has not only not improved, but has lowered the salary increase measures and successively laid off employees of the Electricity and Gas Department, and recruited new employees with lower salaries. Therefore, the situation of the employees being forced is no different from that of the two. The employees are very sympathetic to the workers' declaration of a work slowdown and will not be confused by the company's one-sided notice."

Judges Should Respect Human Rights - Defendants Should Not Be Arbitrarily Detained - The Ministry of Justice Ordered All Provincial High Courts to Comply Yesterday 169

The Ministry of Justice believes that various courts often arbitrarily order bail for defendants who should not be detained, and the accompanying bailiffs take the opportunity to demand and make things difficult. Yesterday, it specially instructed the presidents and chief prosecutors of the high courts of all provinces to comply with the following: in the future, defendants should not be ordered to post bail unless there are special circumstances, and judges must not have the intention of evading responsibility and forgetting the way of human rights. The reporter of the Daily News learned that the original order was as follows: "The case of untried detainees is related to the security of conduct. The National Government has previously issued a clear order, and this Ministry has already issued a circular to comply with it. The so-called bail is a guarantee under the Criminal Procedure Law. Permitting bail and suspending detention should be ordered to pay a security deposit in accordance with the law. However, the amount of the security deposit must be considered carefully and a reasonable amount must be determined. It must not be excessive. It should be allowed to be replaced by valuable securities or a guarantee in accordance with the law. If the relevant valuable securities are submitted, or a guarantee is issued by a person or business with considerable financial resources, it should be approved. According to the provisions of the Criminal Procedure Law, detainees may also be entrusted to their relatives or other appropriate persons without ordering bail, and they may only restrict their residence and suspend detention. Although this order only mentions bail, in the case of untried detainees, the intention of the National Government to sympathize with ordinary prisoners should be fully understood, and it should be handled in a practical manner, without waiting to be said. The measures for suspending detention stipulated by law should be strictly followed, and the implementation of detention for criminal defendants must be carried out with caution. Detention must not be arbitrarily carried out unless there are the circumstances stipulated in Articles 41 to 43 of the Criminal Procedure Law, and it is considered necessary. This is the instruction of this Ministry No. 1438 of this year, which has been repeatedly warned by Liu. Article 86 of the Criminal Procedure Law stipulates that a defendant who does not have the circumstances stipulated in Articles 41 to 43 may also be ordered to post bail or be entrusted, but it clearly states that it is limited to when it is necessary. However, it is found that the courts often abuse this article, and arbitrarily order bail for defendants who should not be detained, regardless of whether it is necessary or not. It is not easy for the defendant to find bail, and the accompanying bailiffs may take the opportunity to demand and make things difficult, so there are those who are illegally detained because they have no bail. This kind of long-standing habit must be thoroughly corrected. In the future, defendants who do not meet the conditions for detention must not be ordered to post bail unless there are special circumstances. When this kind of necessity arises, the method of entrustment should also be considered. Whether the person posting bail or being entrusted is appropriate should be determined by the relevant judicial officer, and must not be completely delegated to the servant. In short, whether the current regulations on detention are properly applied is of great importance to the defendant's freedom rights. As a judicial officer, one must not have the intention of evading responsibility and forgetting the way of respecting human rights." Therefore, this order is given to the President and Chief Prosecutor of the Court for information, and to be relayed to all subordinates for information. This order.

The British, American, and Russian Gasoline War - Car Owners Benefit Greatly 170

The Great Beauty Evening News reported that the gasoline sales war between the British, American, and Russian sides is still continuing. Car owners in this port can still enjoy great benefits. If there are excess sales, the three companies will share them. The Soviet Russian Oil Everywhere Company wants to join this agreement and make the excess sales shared by four companies, so it is putting as much pressure as possible on the three companies to force them to agree. It is currently expected that the three companies will not be able to sustain this price competition for long, so the proceeds from the sale of oil will not be able to cover transportation costs, the interests of distributors, and taxes. The situation is different for Soviet Russia. It is heard that it only charges the Guanghua Company two corners per gallon, and the interests of distributors and taxes are borne by Guanghua. Because Soviet Russia is state-owned, its crude oil cost is only the value of the oil workers, so it is heard that the Oil Everywhere Company is willing to temporarily lose money on oil shipped to China for advertising purposes. It is currently building oil storage tanks in Hankou and is engaging in negotiations to establish distribution centers in Hong Kong. There are more than 25,000 cars in the city.

Foreign Steamer Smashes Cargo Ship - Eighteen Fall into Water - Speeds Away Without Stopping 171

A cargo ship from Xuanzhou, Chaohu, recently loaded 800 dan of wheat bearing the Xie Ji mark in Jiangbei, intending to transport it to Shanghai to deliver it to a flour mill. On the afternoon of the 2nd of this month, as it was sailing past Waisha, Chongming, due to unfavorable winds, it dropped anchor. At that time, a foreign steamer fully loaded with coal came speeding from behind. Upon seeing it, the cargo ship immediately steered towards the shoal to give way and avoid a collision. Unexpectedly, the steamer did not turn its course but continued to sail on. Seeing the steamer approaching, the cargo ship shouted to stop it, but the steamer ignored the warnings and sailed straight on, violently ramming the stern of the cargo ship. The stern was smashed and immediately flooded, and the hull also capsized. The cargo ship cried for help, but the steamer, having caused the accident, still did not stop to provide assistance but increased its speed and sped eastward. The cargo ship had a total of eighteen people on board, including family members and crew, all of whom fell into the water. Fortunately, a Qidong steamer passed by and immediately stopped to provide assistance, rescuing eleven people. The wife and children of the captain were rescued by a pig boat, which transported the rescued wife and children of the captain, along with the crew, to Wusong. The captain discovered that four crew members were still missing. The captain took a train to Shanghai in the afternoon to report the incident, and the flour mill offered to negotiate. According to reports, the steamer had no Chinese characters, and after causing the accident, it did not stop when they cried for help, but continued sailing away. The factory has instructed them to investigate the ships that passed by that day to facilitate negotiations, and is also chartering a ship to inspect whether the cargo can be salvaged. The ship and cargo are valued at 13,000 to 14,000 yuan.

Xuan Ziye Posthumous Dispute - Xuan Qi Accused of Forging Will - Defendant Raises Jurisdiction Issue 177

Xuan Ziye, a wealthy merchant from Gaoyou residing at No. 41 Malong Road, passed away in the winter of 1931. His second wife, Huang, recently accused his eldest son, Xuan Qi, of forging a will in the Second Special District Court. The case was heard by Judge Li Liang in the Seventh Tribunal. The plaintiff was represented by lawyers Zhang Shizhao and E Sen, who stated that the plaintiff married Xuan Ziye as his second wife in 1917 and had two sons and two daughters, all of whom are still young. Xuan Qi was born to the first wife. When Xuan Ziye was dying, he did not make a will. Until August of last year, Xuan Qi suddenly handed Huang a copy of the will, which she found very strange. When she questioned him, the defendant verbally promised to reconcile, but he was insincere. Examining the contents of the will, the defendant, in the position of an heir, in addition to receiving a gift, actually received half of the entire estate, while Xuan Huang and her four children, totaling five shares, only received half of the estate. Moreover, the procedure completely violated legal formalities, which undoubtedly proved that Xuan Qi had forged it after the fact. The defendant Xuan Qi did not appear, and lawyer Gong Yuanbiao appeared on his behalf, stating that the defendant is currently employed at the Nanjing Shanghai Bank and should be under the jurisdiction of the Jiangning Local Court. The plaintiff's lawyer objected and presented many exhibits. After both parties debated once, Judge Li ruled in court that the case should be under the jurisdiction of the Second Special District. The defendant's lawyer then requested a postponement due to issues with his power of attorney, which the court granted, ordering a postponement for further summons.

Essays

— Yong Lin

Urban Youth and Rural Rats 196

— Yin Feng

Urban youths and rural rats are as different as horses and cows, so how can they be compared? Jesus has his reasons, so please see the explanation below...

More affluent farmers are generally unwilling to sell the harvested rice grains in the same year; they always carefully and solemnly store them in the barn to wait for the coming year, because when new rice comes on the market, the price of rice will decline to some extent. Unless they are in urgent need of money, farmers always sell when the price of rice rises. Everyone will use the trade strategy of "selling at a good price." Unexpectedly, in this year of cheap grain and bumper harvest, the price of rice is going from bad to worse, sinking without end, with no hope of rising, making farmers wait more and more wrong. Not only that, but also rats make trouble, intentionally messing things up, so that storing it for one more day means feeding the rats one more meal. In previous years, the storage days were few, and the losses were not significant. This year, the storage days are many, and the losses are greater. Farmers, seeing the two-fold losses - one is the daily decline in the price of rice, and the other is the nightly theft by rats - increasing day by day, might as well sell the rice and change it into foreign money. In addition to "cheap grain hurting farmers," there is also a bad phenomenon of "rats harming farmers," causing farmers to cry out in pain. Rural rats have become the scourge of the countryside.

As for the urban youths - these young masters and modern girls who only know how to waste in every possible way and do not produce even the slightest bit, they squander the money accumulated by their ancestors' blood and sweat, or by taking responsibility, or by scheming, without the slightest care or heartache, as much as possible. They only harm society and do not benefit it. The standard of living is getting higher day by day, their waste is getting greater day by day, and the harm to society is getting deeper day by day, resulting in unimaginable and irreparable consequences. So, the money bags and foreign boxes of the ancestors are like the barns of farmers; the former hopes that the money will gradually increase, and the latter hopes that the price of rice will gradually rise. Unexpectedly, they suffered the same misfortune, not only failing to increase, but also gradually decreasing. Those who steal the rice are the evil rats, and those who use the money are the modern youths; the former reduce the rice grains in the barn, and the latter reduce the money in the money bags and foreign boxes. Rats are the scourge of the countryside, then modern youths are the scourge of the city. Urban youths and rural rats, both are bad things.

Autumn Fan 197

— Xian Xian

Hurricanes, one after another, blew the swaying cicada sounds into silence. Therefore, poets are also like Taoists launching a [Peaceful Public Offering], [not forgetting the season], and [Early Autumn Scenery], [Autumn Sentiment], [Autumn Interest], [Sleepless Autumn Night] and other exquisite words, one after another, jumping out of their throats endlessly. Needless to say, besides those [internal war heroes] with malaria, who can take advantage of this time when people are strong and horses are fat to show off their skills, everyone inevitably has a dejected look towards autumn. You see, therefore, flies, mosquitoes, bedbugs, all of whom are famous for following the powerful, how could one not hide or dodge? The [fan], which was the most prominent in the hot weather, is said to be one of the unfortunates.

In hot weather, the [fan] is truly a blessing to people. When the dog's tongue is two or three inches long, everyone [would rather not eat than be without a fan]. But when the autumn wind rises, [even a big fat man weighing two hundred pounds doesn't have a drop of sweat on him], who still cares about the fan used to attract wind? So silk fans, round fans, silk-mounted fans, brocade-mounted fans, have worked hard all summer, but they have to cry and be put into the box by their masters. As for those cattail fans, oilcloth fans, they have shaken their heads and tails all summer and have already given their all, so at this time, they are thrown into the trash can by their masters, or used for fanning the stove. This is called [Autumn Fan's Donation], which is the most heartbreaking thing.

There are many people in society who have status and are all propped up by others. When they have not yet succeeded, they are naturally very good to those who support them, just like in the hot summer, they are unwilling to let go of the fan even for a moment. Once they are propped up to success, it is as if the weather has dropped from nearly 100 degrees to the 50s or 60s. Seeing the [fan], they feel it is cumbersome, so they throw it away, and the fan is finished. [Even if the autumn fan lies in the trash can crying and wiping tears, or hiding behind the coal stove, raging, it is in vain. The best example is those [founding heroes] of [Manchukuo]. They act as accomplices for the tiger, fabricate public opinion, and try to please their masters in every way, which is like a fan in the hot June, [a gentle breeze], how pleasing. But, be careful, once the summer is over, the weather becomes cooler day by day, and once Japan's [swallowing Manchu plan] matures, the so-called [founding heroes] will inevitably be hidden or thrown away, and there is a danger of becoming a donated [autumn fan].

[Charge! Kill!] 198

— Feng Mouni

This is the military order from the superior officer.

The soldiers, upon hearing the command, all bravely charged forward, not a single one disobeying the order. Why? Because the nation provides them with food and sustains their lives, so they should risk their lives to kill the enemy. Otherwise, without clothes or food, they would still die. It is better to serve the country than to starve to death. They do it for food.

[Perfume—High Heels—Cloth]

This is the order from a lover.

No one who hears the order from a lover dares to disobey. Everyone obeys completely. Even if they have no money to buy it, they will pawn their clothes to do so. Otherwise, the lover will bluntly and impolitely fall in love with someone else. He does it for the lover.

[One bow—Two bows—Three bows]

This is the emcee's command at a wedding.

Anyone getting married is willing to obey the emcee's command. The reason is for the wife, so they would rather bend their backs and waist to bow and dare not disobey the emcee's command.

Going to Yangzhou 199

— Yanqiao

[With ten thousand strings of cash around his waist, he rides a crane to Yangzhou.] Six or seven hundred years ago, poets already had such extravagant hopes. After the embellishment by the salt merchants of the early Qing Dynasty, it naturally became even more touching. Zheng Banqiao said, "Thousands of families raise daughters, teaching them music first; planting flowers for ten miles is like farming the fields." Although it feels a bit excessive, there is at least something symbolic about it. Xu Zhu'an also said, "How could the myriad people know of such extravagant wishes? They all rush to sing 'Spring Breeze' in the style of the infant's babbling. It's pitiful that they have to exchange flawless jade for gold to enrich the old men." I'm afraid this was still a matter of decades ago. Now, the "flawless jade" of Yangzhou, when exchanged for gold, may not be able to make the old men rich. As for the "infant's babbling" that crosses the river to the sea, it is even more unthinkable. The gold they exchange for goes to enrich the fake mothers. Yangzhou! Yangzhou! Isn't it just getting worse and worse?

In my past years, whenever I went to Yangzhou, Nanjing, Biling, or Zhenjiang, I always wanted to visit Yangzhou, but I never could. It wasn't until this year's Qingming Festival that my wish finally came true. From Twelve Forts to the green willow-lined city walls, the car bouncing in the dust made me feel unhappy to begin with. When I arrived at Slender West Lake, although there were crowds of men and women like clouds, the Lama Temple, the Five Pavilion Bridge, Little Jinshan, and Xu Garden were all clearly visible. I truly felt pitifully tired. Only the weeping willows on the opposite bank of the city moat, like loose hair, were more gentle and restrained than the Yangzhou women I saw. A bamboo pole with a makeshift boat resembling a sightseeing boat on Daming Lake was vigorously pushed across the textured water. The boat slowly drifted over, and the gentle breeze awakened my lingering drowsiness. I listened to an old beggar by the shore singing the song "The National Revolution is Successful" while holding out a cloth bag to beg for money. Yangzhou! Yangzhou! — Is he the only one who has grasped the gears of the times?

[Jiangnan looks good from Jiangbei, but once you get to Jiangbei, you regret it]. Enough, enough. At least my diary, which I have kept without interruption for twenty years, has a page about going to Yangzhou.

Sinclair's Sayings 200

— Xiaozhu

The word "success" means money, which also means ease and happiness. The magic of these two words constantly lures all of humanity.

There are three times when people can tell secrets: first, when they are drunk; second, when they are in love; and third, when they are both drunk and in love.

A weakness of humankind is to consider what belongs to others as the best.

Life is all about putting on a show. Once you realize that others are also struggling to put on a show, then you can boldly put on your own show.

The employed class and the employing class have one thing in common: the whip. The handle of the whip is in the hands of the employing class, and the stripes of the whip are on the backs of the working class. This can symbolize the relationship between the two classes forever.

The Four Company Commanders of the Northeast 201

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Sixteen: Bitterness and Sadness Held in the Heart, Blessings Given Before Departure; Busy with Military Affairs, Troops Secretly Moved.

He sat in his own room, thinking blankly. Suddenly, he heard someone outside the door say, "Is Old Zhao in?" As he spoke, the person walked into the room. Then, he clapped his hands and said, "Ha! A volley of guns and cannons brings ten thousand taels of gold." Old Zhao, why do you look so listless? It turned out to be Company Commander Yin Deren, who had walked in. Zhao Ziqiang stood up and smiled, "You are single. Hearing about the departure, you will first not have your meals deducted, and second, get a bit of departure pay. Why wouldn't you be happy?" Yin Deren laughed, "I know, you can't put down that fiancée of yours. What's the big deal? Just take her with you." Zhao Ziqiang said, "Taking a married wife is already a burden. How can I take a fiancée who isn't yet married? Besides, our departure this time is probably to go back and fight in Fengtian. That's no joke. Would they even let us take our families with us to live a comfortable life?" Yin Deren laughed, "So you're here worrying all by yourself, because you can't take your wife with you to fight a war. What's the big deal? Just consider that you haven't gotten engaged to the Yang family girl yet. You're still single, and you'll be free wherever you go. Then there won't be any big problems." Zhao Ziqiang said, "Although that's how you put it, but..." He pondered for a long time, and he couldn't say the sentence. Yin Deren laughed, "People's hearts are made of flesh. You're such a good wife, just about to be in your hands, and now you have to leave her. Tell me, who wouldn't be sad?" Having spoken, he lightly gave a "haha." Zhao Ziqiang said, "I'm not joking. Think, how unfortunate is this situation? The day after I got engaged, there was a separation. First, my father can't bear to part with me. Second, he and the Yang family live in the front and back courtyards, and he can't avoid seeing them morning and night. If he hears any gossip about them, I'm afraid it will make him even more upset in his heart." (207)

Gansu and Ningxia Athletes Arrive in Beijing; Encounter Bandits En Route, Plead Repeatedly, Pay 60 Yuan in Total for Safe Passage 204

— Liaoning Swimming Athletes Arrived in Beijing First —

A total of fifteen athletes from Ningxia and Gansu provinces arrived in Pu at 8:00 AM yesterday morning. The reception team from the organizing committee sent cars to welcome them to the Central Stadium. After completing the registration procedures, they were assigned to the athlete dormitory at Yuan Zi No. 1. According to the team, which departed from Ningxia on September 18, they encountered many bandits at Xishan Mouth, about 800 li away. After repeated negotiations, the bandits saw that they were all poor students without many possessions. The Gansu and Ningxia teams paid a total of 60 yuan, and they were allowed to pass safely. After arriving in Ping, they were stranded for another five or six days and only arrived in Beijing this morning. The province is far away in the border region, and transportation is inconvenient. They felt quite tired after many days en route. Therefore, when reporters visited, they were all sound asleep in the dormitory. It was said that it was easy to come, but it would take at least more than a month to return to the province. The only newspaper in the area is the "Republic Daily" run by the provincial party headquarters, which publishes only two small sheets daily. News from the central government is received via radio broadcasts. The "Shen Bao" and "Xin Wen Bao" newspapers from Shanghai arrive 15 to 20 days later. Since Chairman Ma came to the province, education has been vigorously promoted. There is now one middle school and one normal school, which are combined into one location, with about 300 students. The Second Middle School is under preparation, with only 50 students. In addition, there is a girls' normal school and an attached elementary school with about 100 female students in total. When they set off, it happened to be when the elementary school teachers were on strike due to unpaid salaries. Since school education is like this, there is even less to talk about in terms of sports. Only Wu Jiujiu on this team has relatively good sprinting results. In the Northwest Games, his results were 11.6 seconds for the 100 meters, 22.4 seconds for the 200 meters, and 54 seconds for the 400 meters. It is hard to be sure if he will be able to score points in the future. It was also said that three of the seven members of the team are Muslims. Fortunately, the organizing committee has made preparations for halal food, so there should not be any dietary difficulties.

Gansu: A total of eight people, led by Wang Dehou, secretary Sun Yatian, athletes Yang Junlin, Wang Yuchun, Men Shenglin, Zhang Qian, Zhang Weihui, and Qiang Jingbang. Among them, Zhang Qian's javelin results are better. Zhang Jun participated in the Northwest Games held in Ningxia on the 10th of last month and won first place in the javelin with a result of 34.50 meters.

Liaoning: The athletes Shi Xingteng, Shi Xinglu, and Shi Ruisheng (female) have already arrived yesterday, with Shi Xing serving as the leader. They are all swimming athletes. The remaining athletes are expected to arrive in Beijing this morning. The team is currently residing in rooms 2 and 3 of the Yuan Zi building. The three Shis are all famous swimming experts. The sister of Shi Xinglong proves that they come from a family with a long tradition of scholarship. They are sure to achieve satisfactory results in swimming.

In yesterday's competition, the short-distance results of Wen Jingling of Shanghai University, a National Games athlete from this city, were the most outstanding in the 50-yard and 100-yard freestyle, with a wide gap between him and the second place. The remaining results were average. Fujian Province lacks outstanding talent. Although Wang Honglong won in the long distances, Shanghai University lacks long-distance talent, so there is nothing remarkable about it. Wang's results still need to improve. The Fujian athletes had a high speed in the backstroke event, but they did not know how to turn. Every time they turned, they lost a lot of time. The third place was a Fujian athlete, but he was disqualified for not complying with the turning rules, and the fourth place was promoted. Liu Lingci, the only swimming athlete from the Philippines to attend the National Games, participated in the 200-meter breaststroke as a performance, but ended up in fourth place. The relay race was completed after the lights were turned on.

Free translation is also available, making it one of the features of this conference.

The details are as follows:

Grand Event of the Conference

(1) Opening, (2) Music Playing, (3) Singing the Party Song, (4) Offering the Highest Respect to the Party and National Flags and the Portrait of the Premier, (5) The Chairman Reads the Premier's Will Respectfully, (6) Silence, (7) The Chairman of the Conference Delivers a Speech, (8) The Representative of the Municipal Party Committee Delivers a Speech, (9) The Vice Chairman Reports, (10) Guests Give Speeches, (11) Giving Prizes, (12) Swearing Oath, (13) Music Playing, (14) Photographing, (15) Dismissal

Attendees 219

Included the Mayor's wife, Director Pan of the Municipal Education Bureau, Section Chief Chen, Huang Tiren of the Municipal Party Headquarters, Jin Keying of the Land Bureau, Zheng Xigu, principal of Shanghai Provincial High School, Zhang Qidong of the Chinese Sports Association, Ma Chonggan and Rong Qizhao of the Municipal Games, athletes attending the National Games, and more than 300 award-winning athletes. The Municipal Public Security Bureau Military Band was present to play music. The Municipal Education Bureau sent Shao Rugan, Li Wanyu, Lü Hailan, and Cheng Fengxiang to serve as receptionists.

Director's Address 220

The meeting commenced at two o'clock. The chairman was Director Pan, the emcee was Yuan Zengyu, and the recorders were Ding Shoutang and Chen Guangling. The rituals were duly performed. Mayor Wu was unable to attend due to other engagements, so Director Pan delivered the address on his behalf. He stated, in brief, that today's gathering, holding both the oath-taking ceremony for the city's delegation to the National Games and the awards ceremony for the City Games, is a glorious and solemn occasion. Mayor Wu was unable to attend due to other engagements, so he has sent a representative to deliver the speech. The relationship between sports and the nation is clear to everyone, but it is hoped that everyone will not only pursue their own physical fitness but also use their strength to spread the spirit of valuing sports throughout the country, so that all the people can participate and strengthen their bodies to undertake arduous and difficult tasks. Shanghai occupies an important position in China and should make greater efforts to promote sports. We know that the current situation is extraordinary. In the fifteen years since the European War, the world has experienced first a period of reform, then a period of recovery, and in the last five or six years, a period of intense crisis. All phenomena, and the intensity of competition, have returned to the state before the European War. Scholars who study world issues deeply believe that the outbreak of a second world war is imminent, and it will certainly involve China. When great calamity befalls us, China's land will become a battlefield, its people will become sacrifices on the battlefield, and China's products will be used to supply the needs of the battlefield. In this period, China has only two paths: revival or destruction. If we want to revive, we must prepare for all aspects of a second world war, using manpower to develop land and create wealth, so that at least at that time, we can support resistance on our own land and have a chance of revival. Therefore, the importance of sports is not only for the individual but is related to the survival of the entire nation. You are all strong members of the sports community and will be at the forefront of national sacrifice in the future. In this National Games, it is hoped that first, you will have a spirit of cooperation, taking care of the entire delegation; second, you will uphold sportsmanship, absolutely abide by the regulations and discipline of the conference, and obey commands. Then, even if you do not win medals, you can increase the glory of our city.

Report on Conference Affairs 221

Following this, Ma Chonggan, a member of the City Games Standing Committee, reported briefly that the City Games were held from September 21st to 23rd, and all events have concluded successively. A total of 846 athletes participated in this City Games: 200 in track and field, 67 in national martial arts, 68 in swimming, and 511 in ball games. Many records were broken, both city and national. The cooperation and performance in ball games and national martial arts have also improved significantly compared to the past. Athletes attending the National Games were selected by the selection committee, including 32 male athletes in track and field all-around, 15 in football, 10 in basketball, 12 in volleyball, 15 in baseball, 5 in tennis, 13 in swimming, 10 in national martial arts, 17 female athletes in track and field, 12 in basketball, 15 in volleyball, 15 in softball, 6 in tennis, and 6 in swimming, totaling 183 people. Among them, one person participates in two events, so the actual number is 161. Training began on September 25th and it has now been decided to depart on the morning of the 8th of this month.

Then, Huang Tiren, a representative of the City Party Headquarters, delivered a speech, hoping that everyone would continue to work hard in the future to catch up with the sports achievements of other countries. Next, Guan Zhengxigu spoke, hoping for three points: (1) to promote the spirit of sports, to seek the universal physical development of the people to save the nation from decline and national disasters; (2) to strive for progress, so that achievements increase year by year; (3) to forge physical fitness, to prepare for dealing with world crises. Finally, Rong Qizhao's speech was brief.

This is our oath."

Foreign News

International Mobile Educational Film Measures - China Agrees to Minister Hu Signing the Treaty - Our Country Must Still Retain the Right to Review Films to Prevent Abuses 231

The international convention on international mobile educational film measures and its guarantee implementation measures were sent by the League of Nations to the Chinese Ministry of Foreign Affairs and forwarded to the Ministry of Education for review and approval. As the League of Nations meeting is approaching, our country has sent Minister Hu Shize to attend the meeting regarding educational films. Because the meeting is scheduled to open on October 5th, the draft treaty and measures must be signed. Our country has expressed its approval of the draft treaty, but when educational films produced by various signatory countries apply for exemption from customs duties upon import, our country must still retain the right of inspection to prevent abuses. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs, in response to Minister Hu's telegram requesting instructions from Beijing, has telegraphed the minister to sign the treaty in accordance with the Ministry of Education's review opinion to retain the right of inspection.

The following is an excerpt of the main points of the draft treaty on international circulation of educational films related to education:

The League of Nations' protocol on the international circulation of educational films stipulates that educational films may circulate freely internationally.

The signatory countries, members and non-members of the League of Nations, (1) firmly believe that educational films can enhance mutual understanding between nations and promote military cooperation, which is in line with the purpose of the League of Nations; (2) firmly believe that educational films are an effective tool for promoting progress in intellectual, moral, and physical education, and therefore it is essential to have free circulation internationally; (3) are well aware that educational films are not yet widespread and that the scope of their distribution internationally is too narrow; (4) feel that customs duties are a major obstacle to the popularity of educational films, and that the financial benefits gained by various countries as a result cannot compensate for the educational losses incurred.

Therefore, the following clauses are agreed upon. These clauses aim to clarify the meaning of educational films and to adopt the method of exempting customs duties, so that they can circulate freely internationally (Our country must still retain the right of inspection to prevent abuses). (Article 1) According to the meaning of this treaty, films that conform to educational principles are defined as international educational films: (1) Films that accurately convey news of international organizations recognized by member states of the League of Nations and other countries that have been formally recognized by member states of the League of Nations; (2) Films that are prepared for schools of all levels; (3) Films that aim to provide vocational training, vocational guidance, and for the work of scientific organizations; (4) Films that relate to scientific research or technical research, or aim to promote scientific knowledge; (5) Films that relate to health issues, physical exercise, public welfare, and charitable undertakings. (Article 2) Within six months of the entry into force of this treaty, each signatory country shall, in accordance with the provisions of this treaty, exempt educational films produced by film companies or film organizations within the territory of other signatory countries from customs duties and all surtaxes, except for postage, registration fees, and transportation costs for import and export.

The countries agreed that educational films conforming to one of the following clauses shall be subject to the preceding provision of this article: (1) The negative has been shot and developed; (2) The positive has been shot and printed.

As for sound films, dialogue films, and sound commemorative films, the provisions of this treaty shall also apply.

Each signatory country, in accordance with the provisions of the preceding paragraph of this article, shall further agree that the inland tax on the sale or transfer of educational films produced in other signatory countries shall not exceed the amount collected by the country of origin.

(Article 3) Films applying for exemption from customs duties in accordance with the provisions of this treaty must be sent to the International Educational Film Association for review. If the association recognizes the film as an educational film in accordance with the provisions of Article 1 of this treaty, it may issue a license (omitted below).

(Article 4) (1) If the authorities of the importing country deny that the film is an educational film and reject the request for exemption from customs duties, and the government of the producing country believes that the circulation of the film is very beneficial from the standpoint of a country's culture, then the government of the producing country may kindly inform the government of the importing country, and the two governments shall jointly discuss the issue. (2) (3) Omitted. (4) If the authorities of the importing country believe that the film does not conform to the meaning of education, educational principles, or reject exemption from customs duties for other reasons of public interest, then the preceding articles shall not be cited. (Article 5) (Omitted). (Article 6) This treaty stipulates that it shall not interfere with the laws and regulations of each signatory country regarding the inspection of films, or the plan to crack down on the import or transfer of films for the sake of social security.

(Article 7) For educational films stipulated in accordance with Article 1, each signatory country shall formulate special preferential tax reduction and freight exemption measures.

(Article 8) Within six months of the effective implementation of this treaty, each signatory country shall notify each other and report to the International Educational Film Association of the following two clauses: (1) The names of the organizations that are exempt from customs duties in accordance with Article 3; (2) Detailed measures for implementing the various articles of this treaty.

(Article 10) Omitted. (Article 11) This treaty shall be based on the English and French source texts as the standard. Member states or non-member states of the League of Nations may approve it within six months.

(Article 12) This treaty shall be effective only after ratification. The instruments of ratification shall be deposited with the Secretary-General of the League of Nations, and the Secretary-General shall notify the member states and non-member states of the League of Nations of the deposit and the effective date of the deposit.

(Article 13 Article 14) Omitted. (Article 15) (1) This treaty shall expire three years after the date of its implementation; (2) The expiration of this treaty shall be notified by the signatory country to the Secretary-General of the League of Nations, and the Secretary-General shall notify all member and non-member states of the League of Nations of the notice and the date of receipt of the document; (3) This treaty shall expire one year after the receipt of the notice.

(Article 16) (1) (2) (3) (4) Each clause is omitted. (Article 17) This treaty must be registered by the Secretary-General of the League of Nations before it can be effectively implemented.

The plenipotentiaries of various countries signed this treaty in Geneva. A copy of the signature book is now kept in the archives of the Secretariat of the League of Nations, and after being reproduced in the same way, it will be distributed to the member and non-member states of the League of Nations.

Chinese Film Yearbook - Directory Compilation Committee 232

The Chinese Film Yearbook Directory Compilation Committee held a meeting at the Ministry of Education from 5:00 PM to 9:00 PM on the 4th. The committee members Chen Lifu, Wang Pingling, Li Qinbi, Li Jiaxiang, Dai Ce, and the committee members of the Chinese Educational Film Association Guo Youshou, Peng Baichuan, etc., were present. Techniques, (6) Makeup, (7) Set Design, (8) Cinematography, (9) Sound Engineering, (10) Production Methods, (11) Materials, (12) Censorship)), (L) The Situation of Foreign Film Industry in China ((1) Ministry of Education Issues Regulations on the Qualifications of Civics Teachers and Deans of Students in Secondary Schools 233

The Ministry of Education issued an order to the education departments and bureaus of various provinces and cities on the 4th, stating that "The Executive Yuan's Instruction No. 4547 states, [The National Government's Instruction No. 446 states, [The Central Executive Committee's Letter states, [Upon investigation, regarding the improvement of Party Ideology Education, the Ministry of Education's proposed method for consolidating Party Ideology textbooks for primary and secondary schools was approved by this committee last year. Recently, it was found that the Ministry of Education has issued a notice to all primary and secondary schools across the country to discontinue Party Ideology courses from the first semester of the 22nd year of the Republic of China, and to adopt social textbooks such as Civics, History, and Geography for primary and secondary schools that have been re-edited by the Ministry, which incorporate the Party Ideology of this Party. Although Party Ideology will not be set up as a separate course from now on, the aforementioned subjects such as Civics, History, and Geography are closely related to Party Ideology, and it is still necessary to pay attention to the selection of teachers who are responsible for these courses, especially Civics, which is the most important. Except for primary schools, which do not have a Civics course and do not have full-time teachers, it is necessary to review the qualifications of Civics teachers and deans of students in all secondary schools in accordance with the method of reviewing the qualifications of Party Ideology teachers. Therefore, the Regulations on Reviewing the Qualifications of Civics Teachers in Secondary Schools, the Regulations on Reviewing the Qualifications of Deans of Students in Secondary Schools, and the Organizational Regulations of the Committee for Reviewing the Qualifications of Deans of Students and Civics Teachers have been formulated and submitted to the 86th Standing Committee of this Committee for approval. Furthermore, primary school teachers are related to the enlightenment of children's thinking, and they should all have a correct understanding of the Three Principles of the People. Therefore, it was resolved at the same meeting that primary school teachers should pay attention to their understanding of Party Ideology when they are examined or tested. Except for those who have studied Party Ideology courses at school, they should be examined. If the test results are not good, they should be ordered to take supplementary lessons. The detailed methods will be formulated by the Ministry of Education as soon as possible. In addition to issuing a notice to the party departments of various provinces and cities to comply with it, and abolishing the previously issued Regulations on Reviewing the Qualifications of Party Ideology Teachers, the Regulations on Reviewing the Qualifications of Civics Teachers in Secondary Schools, the Regulations on Reviewing the Qualifications of Deans of Students in Secondary Schools, and the Organizational Regulations of the Committee for Reviewing the Qualifications of Deans of Students and Civics Teachers are attached in one copy each and sent for your records. It is hoped that you will check and forward them to the relevant agencies for compliance.]] etc. Therefore, it should be handled accordingly. Therefore, the original attached regulations are issued so that the said hospital can be transferred to comply with this order.]] etc. In compliance with this, the original attached regulations are copied and issued for the Ministry to comply with. This order, a total of three types of original attached regulations are copied and issued for compliance.

(1) Regulations for the Examination of Civic Instructors in Secondary Schools 234

Adopted by the 86th Standing Committee Meeting of the Fourth Central Executive Committee on August 31, 1933. Article 1: These regulations are formulated in accordance with Article 1 of the "Regulations for the Examination of Deans of Students in Secondary Schools" and Article 1 of the "Regulations for the Examination of Civic Instructors in Secondary Schools." Article 2: The Qualification Examination Committee for Deans of Students and Civic Instructors in provinces or cities (municipalities directly under the Executive Yuan) shall be organized by the provincial or special municipal Party headquarters in conjunction with the highest educational administrative organs of the respective provinces or cities (municipalities directly under the Executive Yuan). The committee shall examine the qualifications of deans of students and civic instructors in the following levels of schools: (1) Provincial, municipal (municipalities directly under the Executive Yuan), or county/city-established secondary schools and private secondary schools approved for establishment; (2) Secondary schools attached to universities or higher vocational schools within the province or city. Article 3: The Qualification Examination Committee for Deans of Students and Civic Instructors in provinces or cities (municipalities directly under the Executive Yuan) shall consist of five to seven members. In addition to the ex-officio members, one being mutually elected from the members of the provincial or special municipal Party headquarters and the other being the head of the educational administration, the remaining members shall be Party members who have graduated from specialized schools or above and possess educational experience, selected and appointed by the provincial or special municipal Party headquarters in conjunction with the local educational administrative organs. Their appointments shall be reported to the Central Mass Movement Guidance Committee and the Ministry of Education for record. Article 4: In areas where no Party headquarters is established, the Party affairs special commissioner shall, in consultation with the local highest educational administrative organ, formulate measures based on the situation and submit them to the Central Mass Movement Guidance Committee for implementation upon approval. Article 5: The Qualification Examination Committee for Deans of Students and Civic Instructors is a permanent organization. Its members shall serve in an honorary capacity. The staff assisting in the examination affairs shall be concurrently held by personnel from the provincial or city (municipality directly under the Executive Yuan) Party headquarters and its highest educational administrative organ. Article 6: If there are any matters not covered in these regulations, the Central Mass Movement Guidance Committee may propose amendments to the Central Executive Committee. Article 7: These regulations shall be implemented upon resolution by the Central Executive Committee.

(2) Regulations for the Examination of Deans of Students in Secondary Schools 235

Adopted by the 86th Standing Committee Meeting of the Fourth Central Executive Committee on August 31, 1933. Article 1: The examination of the qualifications of deans of students in all secondary schools nationwide shall be conducted by the Qualification Examination Committee for Deans of Students and Civic Instructors in accordance with these regulations. The organization of the Qualification Examination Committee for Deans of Students and Civic Instructors shall be determined separately. Article 2: The term "dean of students" as used in these regulations refers to current or prospective deans of students or directors of instruction as stipulated in the regulations for secondary schools. Article 3: All deans of students and directors of instruction in secondary schools nationwide shall be subject to examination by the Qualification Examination Committee for Deans of Students and Civic Instructors. Those who have not been examined or who have failed the examination three months after the Qualification Examination Committee for Deans of Students and Civic Instructors begins its work in their respective locations shall not continue to hold the position. Article 4: Deans of students and directors of instruction in secondary schools nationwide must directly request examination from the Qualification Examination Committee for Deans of Students and Civic Instructors, or the examination may be requested by (1) the respective secondary schools, (2) educational administrative organs at all levels, or (3) Party headquarters at all levels. Article 5: Any Party member (including probationary Party members) or person who has not yet joined the Party but has studied the Three Principles of the People, possesses the qualifications for secondary school teachers stipulated by the educational administrative organs, and has served in secondary school student affairs positions may request to be examined for the qualifications of dean of students in various secondary schools. Article 6: All applicants for examination shall submit the various credentials stipulated in Article 5 of these regulations, as well as the following: 1. Two recent half-length photos; 2. Application form; 3. Curriculum vitae. Article 7: Party members who possess any of the following qualifications may be exempt from examination but must submit documents proving their qualifications to the Qualification Examination Committee for Deans of Students and Civic Instructors for registration. After registration, they shall obtain the qualifications of dean of students in secondary schools: (1) Obtaining a certification or examination certificate as a qualified secondary school dean of students and having at least one year of experience in student affairs work in secondary schools; (2) Having served as a certified Party doctrine teacher or a member of the Qualification Examination Committee for Party Doctrine Teachers and having experience in student affairs work in secondary schools; (3) Currently serving or having served as a member of the Qualification Examination Committee for Deans of Students and Civic Instructors. Article 8: Deans of students who have passed the examination and possess the qualifications stipulated in Article 7 of these regulations shall be issued a qualification certificate by the Qualification Examination Committee for Deans of Students and Civic Instructors. Article 9: In areas where there is a shortage of personnel with the qualifications stipulated in Articles 5 and 7 of these regulations, the respective principals may propose the appointment of individuals who have a clear understanding and belief in Party doctrines, have studied and have experience in student affairs, and possess the qualifications for teachers stipulated by the educational administrative organs. They shall state their reasons to the Qualification Examination Committee for Deans of Students and Civic Instructors for approval as substitute deans of students. Article 10: Before employing a substitute dean of students, each secondary school must submit the substitute dean of student's application form, curriculum vitae, school diploma, or other documents sufficient to prove teacher qualifications, and two recent half-length photos. If they have written works, they should be submitted together for examination and approval. Only after a certificate of substitute dean of students has been issued may they be employed. Article 11: Deans of students and substitute deans of students who have passed the examination may be introduced by two members of the provincial or special municipal Party headquarters on behalf of the Qualification Examination Committee for Deans of Students and Civic Instructors to become probationary Party members. Article 12: After being hired by a school, deans of students and substitute deans of students who have passed the examination shall submit a report on their work situation to the Qualification Examination Committee for Deans of Students and Civic Instructors at least once per semester for assessment. Article 13: If there are any matters not covered in these regulations, the Central Mass Movement Guidance Committee may propose amendments to the Central Executive Committee. Article 14: These regulations shall be implemented upon resolution by the Central Executive Committee.

Regulations for the Examination of Civic Instructors in Secondary Schools 236

Adopted by the 86th Standing Committee Meeting of the Fourth Central Executive Committee on August 31, 1933. Article 1: The examination of the qualifications of civic instructors in all secondary schools nationwide shall be conducted by the Qualification Examination Committee for Deans of Students and Civic Instructors in accordance with these regulations. The organization of the Qualification Examination Committee for Deans of Students and Civic Instructors shall be determined separately. Article 2: The term "civic instructor" as used in these regulations refers to current or prospective teachers of civics courses in secondary schools. Article 3: All civic instructors in secondary schools nationwide shall be subject to examination by the Qualification Examination Committee for Deans of Students and Civic Instructors. Those who have not been examined or who have failed the examination three months after the Qualification Examination Committee for Deans of Students and Civic Instructors begins its work in their respective locations shall not continue to hold the position. Article 4: Civic instructors in secondary schools nationwide must directly request examination from the Qualification Examination Committee for Deans of Students and Civic Instructors, or the examination may be requested by (1) the respective secondary schools, (2) educational administrative organs at all levels, or (3) Party headquarters at all levels. Article 5: Any Party member (including probationary Party members) or person who has not yet joined the Party but has studied the Three Principles of the People, possesses any of the following qualifications may request to be examined for the qualifications of civic instructors in secondary schools: (1) Graduates of specialized schools or above who have studied social sciences; (2) Possesses the qualifications for secondary school teachers stipulated by the educational administrative organs and has taught social science courses; (3) Possesses the qualifications for secondary school teachers stipulated by the educational administrative organs and has studied social sciences in depth and has written works. Article 6: All applicants for examination shall submit the various credentials stipulated in Article 5 of these regulations, as well as the following: 1. Two recent half-length photos; 2. Application form; 3. Curriculum vitae. Article 7: Party members who possess any of the following qualifications may be exempt from examination but must submit documents proving their qualifications to the Qualification Examination Committee for Deans of Students and Civic Instructors for registration. After registration, they shall obtain the qualifications of civic instructors in secondary schools: (1) Obtaining a certification or examination certificate as a qualified secondary school Party school teacher and having at least one year of teaching experience in secondary schools; (2) Former certified Party doctrine teacher or member of the Qualification Examination Committee for Party Doctrine Teachers and has served as a secondary school teacher; (3) Currently serving or having served as a member of the Qualification Examination Committee for Deans of Students and Civic Instructors. Article 8: Civic instructors who have passed the examination and possess the qualifications stipulated in Article 7 of these regulations shall be issued a qualification certificate by the Qualification Examination Committee for Deans of Students and Civic Instructors. Article 9: In areas where there is a shortage of personnel with the qualifications stipulated in Articles 5 and 7 of these regulations, the respective principals may propose the appointment of individuals who have a clear understanding and belief in Party doctrines, have studied and have experience in civic instruction, and possess the qualifications for teachers stipulated by the educational administrative organs. They shall state their reasons to the Qualification Examination Committee for Deans of Students and Civic Instructors for approval as substitute civic instructors. Article 10: Before employing a substitute civic instructor, each secondary school must submit the substitute civic instructor's application form, curriculum vitae, school diploma, or

other documents sufficient to prove teacher qualifications, and two recent half-length photos. If they have written works, they should be submitted together for examination and approval. Only after a certificate of substitute civic instructor has been issued may they be employed. Article 11: Civic instructors and substitute civic instructors who are not Party members but have passed the examination may be introduced by two members of the provincial or special municipal Party headquarters on behalf of the Qualification Examination Committee for Deans of Students and Civic Instructors to become probationary Party members. Article 12: After being hired by a school, civic instructors and substitute civic instructors who have passed the examination shall submit a report on their work situation to the Qualification Examination Committee for Deans of Students and Civic Instructors at least once per semester for assessment. Article 13: If there are any matters not covered in these regulations, the Central Mass Movement Guidance Committee may propose amendments to the Central Executive Committee. Article 14: These regulations shall be implemented upon resolution by the Central Executive Committee.
